    Introduction

    Welcome to AeroMegh API documentation. These documentation are meant to be referred to make requests to our APIs and other cloud APIs.

    Language bindings in Shell, Python, and JavaScript can be found to the right of the API description, and the programming language of the examples can be switched with the tabs in the top right.

    Authentication

    The server accepts a request header Authorization in all of its APIs which must contain the OAuth2.0 access token of the user

    Authorization: Bearer access_token

    Replace access_token with the your OAuth2.0 access token received from the Token API.

    The API server follows the standard OAuth2.0 mechanism for logging its users into the system. To access any part of the system, user is required to present their access token. The access token is generated by logging in through the OAuth2.0 flow.

    To log in, the user must call the Login API first and provide their email and password in the request to verify their identity. If the email and password match in the system, an auth code is generated for the AeroMegh client. This auth code can then be used to request the system for the actual access token via the Token API.

    Login

    curl "${BASE_URL}/login?clientName=AeroMegh&responseType=code"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X POST -d '{
    "username": "user_email",
    "password": "user_password"
  }'

    Make sure to replace user_email with your email address and user_password with your password

    The above request returns a response like this:

    {
  "authCode": "lCVqWFoh"
}

    Description

    The login request requires the user to provide their email and password in the request body like so

    {"username": "user_email", "password": "user_password"}

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/login?clientName=AeroMegh&responseType=code

    Query Paramters

    Paramter Description Example
    clientName Specifies the access token requesting OAuth2.0 client AeroMegh
    responseType Specifies how the response is expected code

    The query paramter clientName must always be AeroMegh when using AeroMegh APIs. This informs the IAM system about the OAuth2.0 client which is requesting the bearer token for the user. This client will be verified using the client's Client Credentials in the APIs that come later in the login flow.

    The query paramter responseType specifies that the API must intercept the automated flow of OAuth2.0 login (login -> redirect to client -> request token -> redirect to client) and to send the authentication code for the user immediately in the response of the login API.

    Replace user_email with your email address and user_password with your password

    HTTP Response

    A valid request like the above returns a JSON object in the API response containing one property: authCode. The value of this property is the 8 alphabetic character OAuth2.0 authentication code generated for the user and the client name AeroMegh.

    { "authCode": "lCVqWFoh" }

    Token

    

    curl "${BASE_URL}/token?code=auth_code"
  -H "Authorization: Basic SUFNQWVybzpyQm95YnVlRUZzTE1CMEQwT0dRTw=="
  -X GET

    Make sure to replace auth_code with your authentication code received from the login API

    The above request returns a response like this:

    {
  "username": "email address of the user",
  "access_token": "access token of the user",
  "expires": "Timestamp of the instant when the access token expires",
}

    Description

    The Token API is used to receive the user access token in return for client credentials and the auth code received from the login API

    This API requires the Authorization header to be of type Basic. The standard HTTP Basic authorization mode is a username-password pair string encoded in base64 format. In the Token API the Basic authorization credentials are the client credentails: client_name for username and client_secret for password

    When logging into the AeroMegh server, the following static client credentails are to be used

    Key Value
    client_name AeroMegh
    client_secret rBoybueEFsLMB0D0OGQO

    Which means that when the client credentials are to be sent manually, the following string must be encoded in base64 format and sent in Authorization header preceded by the auth mode name - Basic

    AeroMegh:rBoybueEFsLMB0D0OGQO

    Therefore, the final Authorization header to be sent becomes

    "Authorization" : "Basic SUFNQWVybzpyQm95YnVlRUZzTE1CMEQwT0dRTw=="

    HTTP Request

    GET ${BASE_URL}/token?code=auth_code

    Query Paramters

    Paramter Description Example
    code Auth code received from the login API lCVqWFoh
    Replace auth_code with the authentication code received from the login API

    HTTP Response

    A valid request for the Token API returns a response containing a JSON object as follows
    { "username": "john.doe@gmail.com", "access_token": "8de15782-4f70-45a6-8a61-6f11c60c8044", "expires": "2023-07-27T18:21:07.345Z", }
    In the response object, the requesting client gets 3 paramters, username, access_token and expires.

    Paramter Description
    username Contains the email address of the user
    access_token The UUIDv4 format access token of the user
    expires The ISO String version timestamp of the instance when the access token shall expire.

    Logout

    curl "${BASE_URL}/logout"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -X GET

    Description

    AeroMegh exposes a logout feature on user's request that can be called from any route handler which needs to terminate a login session.

    HTTP Request

    GET ${BASE_URL}/logout

    HTTP Response

    A valid request to logout API terminate login seesion and redirect to the login page.

    Create User

       curl "${BASE_URL}/signup"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X POST -D `{
    "user": {
        "email": " user_email",
        "first_name": "user_firstname",
        "last_name": "user_lastname",
        "phone": "user_phone",
        "password": "user_password",
        "address": "user_address"
    },
    "companyName": "user_companyname",
    "registrationType": "user_registrationtype"

  }`

    Make sure to replace access_token with your access token, user_email,user_firstname,user_lastname,user_phone,user_password,user_address,user_companyname,user_registrationtypewith your email,first_name,last_name,phone,password,address,companyName,registratrionType. 

    
{
    "message": "OK"
}

    Description

    When a user do not have an account and user sign in their account at that time this API will call.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/signup

    HTTP Response

    The response of above API in the form of json body

    { "message": "OK" }

    Send OTP

       curl "${BASE_URL}/sendOTP"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X POST -D `{

    "username":"curtis.howard@mailinator.com"

  }`

    Make sure to replace access_token with your access token, curtis.howard@mailinator.comwith your username. 

    {
    "messsage": "OTP sent to curtis.howard@mailinator.com"
}

    Description

    The sendOTP API send OTP for verify to users email id for two step authentication purpose.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/sendOTP

    Replace curtis.howard@mailinator.com with your registered email address.

    HTTP Response

    A valid request to sendOTP API returns the following json body

    { "messsage": "OTP sent to curtis.howard@mailinator.com" }

    Verify OTP

    javascript

    curl "${BASE_URL}/verifyOTP"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -X GET

    {
    "verification": 0
}

    Description

    When the user sign in to AeroMegh then the AeroMegh site sendOTP on user's registered email to verify their email by using above API

    HTTP Request

    GET ${BASE_URL}/verifyOTP

    HTTP Response

    If above API return the following response in the form of json body then the OTP is not correct.

    { "verification": 0 }

    If above API return the following response in the form of json body then the OTP is correct.

    { "verification": 1 }

    Forget Password API

    curl "${BASE_URL}/requestPasswordResetLink"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X POST -D`{
     "email":"curtis.howard@mailinator.com"
       }`

    Make sure to replace access_token with your access token, curtis.howard@mailinator.com with your registered email. 

    {
   "message": "Password reset link has been sent"
}

    Description

    When the user forget their password they can get their new password with the help of forget password API.The above API sent the link on their registered email id,after activate link user will get new password.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/requestPasswordResetLink

    Replace curtis.howard@mailinator.com with the your registered email.

    HTTP Response

    A above valid request to forgot password API returns the following response

    { "message": "Password reset link has been sent" }

    Check Drone Registration Status AeroGCS Vanilla

       curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/CheckDroneRegistration/:droneID/:droneName"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -X GET

    Make sure to replace :droneID with your drone ID and :droneName with your drone's name.

    Description

    This API is to be called by the AeroGCS Vanilla when a user connects the drone to the GCS software. Along with the API, the GCS must send the Drone ID, Drone Name and the users access token. This data is verified against the database and checked if the drone exists in the system.

    In case the drone exists in the system, the API simply responds saying that the drone exists in the system. Additionally, the Drone Name sent in the request will be updated in the system for the given Drone ID.

    In case the Drone ID does not exist in the system for the user, user's subscription plan will be checked and it will be confirmed whether the user is allowed to add any more drones under his/her account. If yes, the drone is added and suitable response is given. Otherwise, the API throws a 403 code with an error reading that the drone cannot be added since the user's account's drone registration limit has been reached.

    HTTP Request

    GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/CheckDroneRegistration/:droneID/:droneName

    The request generates the following responses

    // Status: 201
{
  "message": "Drone has been registered"
}
// Status: 200
{
  "message": "Drone exists in system"
}
// Status: 202
{
  "message": "The user is not subscribed to any active plan."
}
// Status: 203
{
  "message": "User has exceeded drone usage limit."
}

    AeroMegh

    Get Projects Data

      curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/getProjectData/project/
          "project-name"/"project-id"
    -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
    -H "Content-Type: application/json"
    -X GET

    A successful call to this API will return following response with response code 200.

    
        {
          "flights" : []
          "flight_schedules" : []
          "videos" : []
          "tasks" :[]
          "annotation_sets" : []
          "images" : []
          "image_collections" : []
          "flight_logs" : []
          "plans" :[]
        } //Each Array includes objects of pariticular id's.

    Description

    This API is used to get all projects data with its id's to perform action on particular data like deleting plans or collection from that project.

    HTTP Request

    GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/getProjectData/project/"project-name"/"project-id"

    HTTP Response

    Case Response Status Code Response Body
    Internal server error 500 {message: "An internal error has occured"}
    get project data successfull 200 output given right side

    Delete Projects Data

      curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/deleteProjectData
    -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
    -H "Content-Type: application/json"
    -X DELETE
    BODY
      {
    "type": "tasks/plans/imageCollections/flights....",
    "data": [{
              "id" : "8212d61e8a744e01ab6ac557a422e6e"  
              }]//array of objects which conatains id's of type which want to delete.You will get this data using getProjectsData API.
    
      }

    A successful call to this API will return following response with response code 200.

    
        {
          "deleted" : true,
          "message": "data deleted successfully"
        }

    Description

    This API is used to delete data from project,you have to pass type of data like plans/collections AND array of object which contains id's of type you pass.

    HTTP Request

    DELETE ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/deleteProjectData

    HTTP Response

    Case Response Status Code Response Body
    Internal server error 500 {message: "An internal error has occured"}
    data deleted successfully 200 output given right side

    Covid-19

    Social Distancing API

    

    # With shell, you can just pass the correct header with each request
curl "${BASE_URL}/aeroCloud/detection/detectSocialDistancing"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "apikey: api_key"
  -X POST -d '{"imageurl":"image_url"}'

    Make sure to replace access_token with your access token, api_key with your API key and imageURL with your imageURL to run detection on

    The above request returns a response like this if social distancing is followed:

    {
   "result": {
    "code": 1,
    "message": "Social Distancing is followed",
    "personsDetected": 3
  }
}

    The above request returns a response like this if social distancing is not followed:

    {
  "result": {
    "code": 0,
    "message": "Social Distancing is NOT followed",
    "personsDetected": 3
  }
}

    Description

    The Social Distancing API performs analysis of an image submitted and returns data stating if social distancing was followed as per norms of not.

    The input image must be given via application/json with key image

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/aeroCloud/detection/detectSocialDistancing

    Replace imageURL with the your imageURL.

    HTTP Response

    A valid request to the Social Distancing API returns a JSON response in the following format

    { "result": { "code": 1, "message": "Social Distancing is followed", "personsDetected": 3 } }

    The response object contains one property result which is a JSON object. the result object contains the following properties

    Property Description
    code Integer property. Contains either 0 or 1. 0 indicates that social distancing is not followed and 1 indicates that social distancing has been followed
    message String property. Contains "Social Distancing is followed" or "Social Distancing is NOT followed" when social distancing is followed and not followed respectively
    personsDetected Integer property containing the count of the number of humans detected in the image.

    Crowd Detection API

    

    curl "${BASE_URL}/aeroCloud/detection/detectCrowd"
   -H "Content-Type: application/json"
   -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
    -H "apikey: api_key"
    -X POST   -d '{"imageURL":"image_URL"}'

    Make sure to replace access_token with your access token, api_key with your API key and imageURL with your imageURL to run detection on.

    The above request returns a response like this:

    {
  "headCount": 6
}

    Description

    The Crowd Detection API performs analysis of an image submitted and returns crowd data

    The input image must be given via application/json with key imageurl

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/aeroCloud/detection/detectCrowd

    Replace imageURL with your imageURL.

    HTTP Response

    A valid request to the Crowd Detection API returns a JSON object in the following format

    { "headCount": 6 }

    The response JSON object contains a single property named headCount which is a Integer indicating the number of humans found in the input image

    Masks Detection API

    

    curl "${BASE_URL}/aeroCloud/detection/detectMasks"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
   -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "apikey: api_key"
  -X POST   -d '{"imageURL":"image_URL"}'

    Make sure to replace access_token with your access token, api_key with your API key and imageURL with your imageURL to run detection on.

    The above request returns a response like this:

    {
  "totalDetections": 5,
  "masksDetected": 3,
  "nomaskDetected": 2
}

    Description

    The Mask Detection API performs analysis of an image and finds out if humans are present in the image and returns the statistic about how many of them are wearing a mask.

    The input image must be given via applicatio/json with key imageurl

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/aeroCloud/detection/detectMasks

    Replace imageURL with your imageURL.

    HTTP Response

    A valid request to the mask detection API returns the following JSON object in the response body

    { "totalDetections": 5, "masksDetected": 3, "nomaskDetected": 2 }

    The reponse body JSON object contains the following 3 properties

    Property Description
    masksDetected Number of people wearing a mask in the input image
    nomaskDetected Number of people who are not wearing a mask in the input image
    totalDetections Total number of people in the input image

    Send new service request mail 

      curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/requestNewService/:s_name"
    -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
    -H "Content-Type: application/json"
    -X GET

    A successful call to this API will return following response with response code 200.

    
        {
          "Message": "Email sent successfully."
        }

    Description

    This API is called when a user request for a service.A notification mail will then be sent to services@aeromegh.com, informing of the user, requested service. It will take service name of the service requested by the user as parameter in URL.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/requestNewService/:s_name

    HTTP Response

    Case Response Status Code Response Body
    Internal server error 500 {message: "An internal error has occured"}
    Image uploded successfully 200 {"Message": "Email sent successfully."}

    -X POST
    --body 
      {
          "task_id": "3e029302-9cf9-4c82-b61c-90ac183e899e",
          "algorithm_type":"NDVIB",
          "filter_type":"RGN",
          "min" : -0.44 ,
          "max" : -1.8333
      }

    A successful call to this API will return following response with response code 201.

    
        {
           "message": "Report added successfully"
        }

    Description

    This API is used to save the dronenaksha image layer report

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroFarm/addDNReport"

    HTTP Response

    Response codes explanation:

    Code Details
    500 Internal server has occured (database error).
    202 Invalid task Id
    400 Request is missing some parameter
    409 Report with the same data already generated for this task.
    201 {"message": "Report added successfully"}

"body":

    "username": "xyz@gmial.com"
    "password: "1425367889"
  }

    500 An internal server error has occured.(Datatable related spcific message)
    403 Invalid access token.
    400 Request missing parameters/ Authorization mode must be bearer.
    202 You have already shared assets with this user.
    201 Successful response

When share access to any collection is removed all the other access given under perticular project will also get removed. So to get the overall idea of which accesses are going to remove, this API will be called. It will take project_id, shared_id and email to which data is shared as input.

    Teams

    Invite user to team

      curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroGCSEnterprise/inviteUser"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X POST
  -D
  "body": 
    {
    "user_name": "curtis.howard@mailinator.com",
    "team_id": "2a062914-7ca4-4773-b904-de630c70d827"
    }

    A successful call to this API will return following response with response code 202.

    
  {
    "Message": "User has been sent the inv link."
  }

    Description

    This API is called when an AeroMegh user sends an invite to another user to join their team. This API handles various conditions such as if the team to which he is invited is a valid or not, then if the invite is valid or expired, then if invites are sent to the same user to join the same team with in a week, also all sorts of duplicate entries are validated. Once all the checks are validated, the user will receive an email containing the link to accpet the teams invite.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroGCSEnterprise/inviteUser

    HTTP Response

    Case Response Status Code Response Body
    Internal server error 500 {message: "An internal error has occured"}
    User is already an active member of your team. 409 {message: "The user you are inviting is already an active member of your team."}
    Cannot send multiple invites to same user within a week. 409 {message: "You can not send multiple invites to same user within a week."}
    Team not found in system. 404 {Error : "Team not found"}
    User has been sent the invite link. 201 { "message": "User has been sent the invite link." }

    Accept Invite

    Invite user to team

      curl "${BASE_URL}/acceptInv?inv=cd8a94c7-81a5-445d-92d9-a018bfac5b02"

    Description

    When this API is called, it will first check if the invite is a valid or not, then it will check if the invite is expired or not. And once the invite validation is done, depending on the user type the user will be directed to an HTML page which will contain either login or signup URL.

    HTTP Request

    GET ${BASE_URL}/acceptInv?inv=inviteCode

    Query Paramters

    Paramter Description Example
    inv Specifies the invite id (uuid) of the user invite. cd8a94c7-81a5-445d-92d9-a018bfac5b02

    A successful call to this API will return following response with response code 202.

    
  {
    "Message": "Thank you for accepting the invite.Click here to (hyperlink) login/signup"
  }

    The query paramter inv must always be a valid invite id.

    HTTP Response

    Case Response Status Code Response Body
    Internal server error 500 {message: "An internal error has occured"}
    Invite id invalid/not found 404 {message: "Invite id is invalid/not found"}
    Expired invite id. 400 {message: "Your invite link is expired."}
    User accepts the invite. 202 { "message":Thank you for accepting the invite, click here to (hyperlink)login/signup." }

"message": "OK"
}

    Description

    The edit team plan API is called from GCS to create or update a plan under a certain project.The API has similar data input in body of HTTP request. The format is specified in the right side section.

    If the a new plan is being created, then the API will check if the user is owner or not(check access).If the plan is new it will create a new plan with the details provided in the request body, else it will update an existing plan with the data received in request body.

    This newly created plan or updated plan changes will be reflected on both GCS and server side.

    HTTP Request

    API: POST ${BASE_URL}/Aeromegh/remoteMission/editTeamPlan"

    Body: <Refer right side section>

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <bearer_token>"

    HTTP Response

    A valid request to the edi Team plan API returns a JSON object in the following format

    Case Response Status Code Response Body
    Internal server error. 500 {message: "An internal error has occured"}
    Missing body parameters. 400 {message: "Request missing ______","Authorization mode should be bearer."}
    No team Found. 404 {message: "No teams found for user."}
    Invalid access token. 403 {message: "Invalid access token."}
    Successful call - New plan creted. 200 { message : "Plan created successfully." }
    Successful call - Existing plan updated. 201 { message : "OK." }

    Add/Update Access Permission

    Add/Update Access Permission to a plan

      curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroGCSEnterprise/addUpdatePlanAccess"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X POST
  -D
  "body": 
    {
    "plan_id": "0d1d6b50-b556-4b1d-ad27-111b3d378cbd",
    "team_id": "722eb5ed-1699-46f6-a83e-6360c2912631",
    "username": "aakashgovardhane@gmail.com",
    "permission_id": "55a106a9-f5ee-4c8e-b03a-1c51fa65ba24",
    }

    A successful call to this API will return following response with response code 200.

    
    {
      "Message": "Access permission added"/"Access permission added"
    }

    Description

    This API is called,When admin/project manager wants to add or update access permission of plan to a team member. if user has existing permission then it will be updated and if there is no any existing permission then new entry will be added .

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroGCSEnterprise/addUpdatePlanAccess

    Body: <Refer right side section>

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <bearer_token>"

    HTTP Response

    Case Response Status Code Response Body
    Internal server error 500 {message: "An internal error has occured", error:{errorObject}}
    Acces Permission Added 200 {message: "Access permission added"/"Access permission updated"}
    if user who is requesting is not an owner of the team 403 {message: "FORBIDDEN : You can not delete user because you are not team owner"}

    Get team members

    Get team members of particular team

      curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroGCSEnterprise/getTeamMembers/722eb5ed-1699-46f6-a83e-6360c2912631"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X GET
  -D

    A successful call to this API will return following response with response code 200.

    
    {
      "teamMembers": [
         {
           username: aakashgovardhane@gmail.com,
					 userFullName: Aakash Govardhane,
					 avatarUrl: avatar_url,
					 roleTitle: Pilot,
					 status: Active
         }, //image url and full name is available for only active user. this result is available for all team members.
         {
           username: suraj@gmail.com,
					 userFullName: suraj@gmail.com,
					 avatarUrl: null,
					 roleTitle: Pilot,
					 status: Inactive
        } ////image url and full name is not available for inactive user result  and this result is available only for owner of team.
      ]
    }

    Description

    This API is used to get all team members of particular team.You have to pass only team id through params.and successfully api returns team members.if team member is not active user then avatar_url and full name is not return instead of that null value and username is ruturn respecitively.full name and img url is available only for active status users.Also when this API is called if the user is owner of the team then the result will include all the team members irrespective of their member status, otherwise the result will include only active members of the team.

    HTTP Request

    GET: ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroGCSEnterprise/getTeamMembers/team_id

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <bearer_token>"

    HTTP Response

    Case Response Status Code Response Body
    Internal server error 500 {message: "An internal error has occured"}
    Team members fetched successfully. 200 { "teamMembers": [ { username: aakashgovardhane@gmail.com, userFullName: Aakash Govardhane, avatarUrl: avatar_url, roleTitle: Pilot, status: Active }, //image url and full name is available for only active user. this result is available for all team members. { username: suraj@gmail.com, userFullName: suraj@gmail.com, avatarUrl: null, roleTitle: Pilot, status: Inactive } ////image url and full name is not available for inactive user and this result is available only for owner of team. ] }

    Delete User

    Delete particular user from team

      curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroGCSEnterprise/deleteMember"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X DELETE
  -D
  "body": 
    {
    "team_id": "722eb5ed-1699-46f6-a83e-6360c2912631",
    "username": "aakashgovardhane@gmail.com"
    }

    A successful call to this API will return following response with response code 200.

    
    {
      "Message": "User Deleted successfully from team"
    }

    Description

    This API is called,When admin/project manager wants to delete user from team.if user who is requesting is not an owner of the team,then user will not be deleted.

    HTTP Request

    DELETE ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroGCSEnterprise/deleteMember

    Body: <Refer right side section>

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <bearer_token>"

    HTTP Response

    Case Response Status Code Response Body
    Internal server error 500 {message: "An internal error has occured", error:{errorObject}}
    User Deleted Successfully 200 {message: "User Deleted successfully from team"}
    User not found in team to delete 404 {message: "User could not be found."}
    if user who is requesting is not an owner of the team 403 {message: "FORBIDDEN : You can not delete user because you are not team owner"}

    remove permission access

    remove permisssion access of plan

      curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroGCSEnterprise/removePlanAccess"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X DELETE
  -D
  "body": 
    {
    "team_id": "722eb5ed-1699-46f6-a83e-6360c2912631",
    "username": "aakashgovardhane@gmail.com",
    "plan_id": ">"819d642d-25fd-4393-9026-ae1c0f683e7c
    }

    A successful call to this API will return following response with response code 200.

    
    {
      "Message": "Access removed Successfully"
    }

    Description

    This API is called,When admin/project manager wants to remove access of user from particular plan.You have to pass plan_id,username,and team_id from body.

    HTTP Request

    DELETE ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroGCSEnterprise/removePlanAccess

    Body: <Refer right side section>

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <bearer_token>"

    HTTP Response

    Case Response Status Code Response Body
    Internal server error 500 {message: "An internal error has occured", error:{errorObject}}
    user removed successfully 200 {message: "Access removed Successfully"}
    if user who is requesting is not an owner of the team 403 {message: "FORBIDDEN : You can not remove access of user because you are not team owner"}

    Description

    This API is used to get task details on the task executer. Make sure to replace the taskId with the actual task_id of the task which data is to be retrieved. It will return all task specific details depending on the task type.

    HTTP Request

    HTTP Response

    Response codes explanation:

    Code Details
    500 Internal server has occured (database error).
    403 You are not authorized to access this resource
    400 Request missing some parameter/Invlaid task/Task does not exists.
    200 Result shown on the right side.

   -D
   "body": 
   {
          "user_id": "722eb5ed-1699-46f6-a83e-6360c2912631",
          "detector_id": "4ec11e14-9adc-40c9-9d61-9cb8246bdb8a",
          "name": "testDetector657"
          "display_name": "Test Detector4"
          "task_id: "fb6baaf4-8a6b-4cb5-9fc7-53cc663efacb"
          "objects": "{ object1, object2, obejct3 }"
   }

    A successful call to this API will return following with response code 200.

    
          {
            "message": "Detector added."
          }

    Description

    This API is used to save the detector data. Once a training task is completed, this API shall be called to save the detector data into database under the user.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/PicStork/taskExecuter/saveDetector

    HTTP Response

    Response codes explanation:

    Code Details
    500 Internal server has occured (database error).
    403 Invalid access token
    400 Request missing some parameter.
    202 Detector id duplication./A detector with same name already exists under this user.
    200 Detector added.

    Project Sync

    Project Sync API

     curl "${BASE_URL}/aeroCloud/projectSync"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X POST -D`

  {
  "team_id" : "b1b110c5-159e-4ab7-bcc4-25977c97c1d6",
  "metadata": [
    {
    "path": "./asddfg/GeneralProjectSettings.json",
    "modified": "Fri, 10 Apr 2020 10:18:11 GMT",
    "deleted": "0",
    "cloudLink": "https://pdrlimage.blob.core.windows.net/container1/AeroGCSWorkspace/asddfg/GeneralProjectSettings.json",
    "checksum": "123456hgf"
    }
    ]
}`

      {
  "storage_details" :  [
        {
            "id": "container1",
             "st": "sp=racwdl&st=2020-09-04T09:38:03Z&se=2023-01-05T09:38:00Z&sv=2019-12-12&sr=c&sig=wKvhwiDbaJW6Xc9o0w%2BZBqaSP1eUvYN4Rc3B6rq4IXo%3D"
        }
  ],
  "upSync": [
        {
              "path": "./asddfg/GeneralProjectSettings.json",
              "modified": "Fri, 10 Apr 2020 10:18:11 GMT",
            "deleted": 0,
            "cloudLink": "https://pdrlimage.blob.core.windows.net/container1/AeroGCSWorkspace/asddfg/GeneralProjectSettings.json",
            "checksum": "123456hgf"
        }
    ],
    "downSync": [],
    "toDelete": []
}

    Description

    The sync API requires the AeroGCS software to maintain a record of all the files present in the project workspace of the user. The format of the record of all the files is given in above as the body of the sync API request. It is a list of objects where each object represents a file in the workspace. Each file object contains these parameters:

    1.Path

    Path of the file relative to the root folder of the project workspace of the GCS software along with the file name and extension.

    2.Checksum

    An MD5 checksum of the file

    3.Modified

    A timestamp of the instance when the file was last modified by the GCS software

    4.Deleted

    Whenever a file is deleted by the user through the GCS, the entry of the file is not removed from the files record. It is simply marked as deleted by turning the deleted flag of the file to “true”. At the time of the next project sync, this flag indicates that the file has been deleted from the GCS and so the file and its entry must also be deleted from the cloud. Once the response of this request has been successfully received by the GCS, the GCS must remove the entry of the file from its local record.

    5.CloudLink

    The URL of file in the blob storage of the user if the file has been uploaded to the cloud storage.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/aeroCloud/projectSync

    HTTP Response

    A above API returns following response

    Case Response Status Code Response Body
    Internal server error. 500 {message: "An internal error has occured"}
    No teams found for user. 404 {message: "No team found."}
    Missing body parameters. 400 {message: "Request missing ______","Authorization mode should be bearer."}
    Invalid access token. 403 {message: "Invalid access token."}
    No plans found for user. 204 { storageDetails :[], upSync :[], downSync:[], toDelete:[] }
    User subscription plan check 202 { The user is not subscribed to any active plan. }
    Successful call. 200 { Complete user profile as shown on the right }

    UploadACK API

    curl "${BASE_URL}/aeroCloud/uploadAck"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X POST -D
  `{
  "metadata": [
    {
    "path": "./asddfg/GeneralProjectSettings.json",
    "modified": "Fri, 10 Apr 2020 10:18:11 GMT",
    "deleted": "0",
    "cloudLink": "https://pdrlimage.blob.core.windows.net/container1/AeroGCSWorkspace/asddfg/GeneralProjectSettings.json",
    "checksum": "123456hgf"
    }
    ]
}`

    {
"message": "OK"
}

    Description

    The body of the request of this API contains the same files list as the previous API. The only difference is that this list is simply the list of files which have been newly uploaded to the cloud storage by the GCS software.

    The cloud server updates its record of the files list according to the list received in the body of the API of the new files which have been uploaded to the cloud storage bucket.

    HTTP Request

    ${BASE_URL}/aeroCloud/uploadAck

    HTTP Response

    A valid request to the Upload ACK API returns a JSON object in the following format

    { "message": "OK" }

    Description

    The Create project API is called to create a project and create files in object storage container. The API takes all the required data in the request body in the format specified in the right side section.

    The server then creates appropriate files and folders in the user's object storage container and populates them according to the received configuration.

    This project can then be seen in AeroGCS after API is successfully hit.

    HTTP Request

    API: POST ${BASE_URL}/Aeromegh/AeroGCS/createProject"

    Body: <Refer right side section>

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <bearer_token>"

    A valid request to the Create Project and Plan API returns a JSON object in the following format

    Case Response Status Code Response Body
    Missing body parameters. 400 {message: "Request missing ______","Authorization mode should be bearer."}
    No teams 400 {message: "Request missing ______","Authorization mode should be bearer."}
    Invalid access token. 403 {message: "Invalid access token."}
    Internal server error. 500 {message: "An internal error has occured"}
    Successful call. 200 { success : "true" }

  }

      {
    "message": "Project doesn't already exist"
  }

                "geofence Y": 0.000401,
                "geofence Z": 43
            }

            }

                "geofence Z": 43
            }

    ],
    "Assets": {
      "planMap.png": "http://167.71.238.142:4173/file/46be9f5a-ede9-41bf-a63f-afe630a5679d.png"
    }
  }`

    A valid request to the Create Plan API returns a JSON object in the following format 

    {
"message": "OK"
}

    Description

    The Create Plan API is called to create a plan under a project for a user and create files in object storage container. The API takes all the required data in the request body in the format specified in the right side section.

    The server then creates appropriate files and folders in the user's object storage container and populates them according to the received configuration.

    This project can then be seen in AeroGCS after the next sync cycle.

    HTTP Request

    API: POST ${BASE_URL}/Aeromegh/remoteMission/addPlan

    Body: <Refer right side section>

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <bearer_token>"

    HTTP Response

    A valid request to the Create Plan API returns a JSON object in the following format

    { "message": "OK" }

       curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/support
        -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
        -X POST
        --body '{
          "email":"support1@mailinator.com",
          "enable" : false
        }'
      
     
          A susccessful response with status code 201 :

        {
          message : "Added new support email successfully !"
        }

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/support

    HTTP Response

    { message : "Added new support email successfully !",}

    Response codes explanation:

    Code Details
    500 An internal server error has occured.(Datatable related specific message)
    403 Invalid access token.
    400 Request missing parameters
    202 { message : "Email already exists"}
    201 { message : "Added new support email successfully !"}

    500 An internal server error has occured.(Datatable related specific message)

    202 { message: "Support email does not exist" }
    200 { message: "Support email enabled/disabled" }

    Verify OTP API for android

       curl "${BASE_URL}/ml/phoneVerification/verifyOTP/1234567890/417430/0
      -H 
      -X POST

      "body": 
      {
        "requestType": "0",
        "otp": "123422"
        "phone": 1234567890
      }

      
     
          A susccessful response with status code 200 :
          {
            "message": "OTP verification was successful."
          }

    Description

    This API will be used for otp verification process of android application. It will take registered phone no and otp as body parameter.Also it will take a flag as 0 or 1, which will indicate for which process the OTP is being verified, 0 is for signup, 1 is for login.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/ml/phoneVerification/verifyOTP

    HTTP Response

    A susccessful request to the above API returns a successful message with status code 200

    { "message": "OTP verification was successful." }

    Response codes explanation:

    Code Details
    500 An internal server error has occured.(Datatable related specific message)
    401 OTP expired/Invalid OTP.
    400 Request missing parameters.
    200 OTP verification was successful.

    Add new subscription plan

       curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/SubModule/addNewSubPlan"
-H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
-X POST

      {
    "plan_name": "AeroGCS Enterprise Business",
    "description": "This is Enterprise Plan",
    "service_id": "36006c17-8de7-4c21-9226-13dc29fcf6e3",
    "status": "Active",
    "cost": "999",
    "discount": 0,
  }

    A successful call to this API will return following response with response code 200.

    
            {
                "message": "New subscription plan added.",
                "data": {
                    "id": "1a5e250b-8b86-4a72-b145-f844ba1809b3",
                    "plan_name": "AeroGCS Enterprise Business",
                    "created_date": "2022-02-04T05:30:34.883Z",
                    "plan_type": null,
                    "status": "Active",
                    "plan_cost": "999.00",
                    "price_id": null,
                    "service_id": "36006c17-8de7-4c21-9226-13dc29fcf6e3",
                    "description": "This is Enterprise Plan",
                    "discount": "0"
                }
            }
    }

    Description

    This API will add a new subscription plan. This will be used by admin only. This API will take plan_name, status and service_id as an input.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/SubModule/addNewSubPlan

    HTTP Response

    Response codes explanation:

    Code Details
    500 An internal server error has occured.(Datatable related spcific message)
    403 Invalid access token.
    400 Request missing parameters/ Authorization mode must be bearer.
    409 There is already a subscription plan with the same name."

    Buy Subscription

      curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/user/pgSubscription"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X POST 
  -D
{
  "pg_subscription_plan_id": "f89babcf-a9bf-4213-9bb1-d6b7576e99fd",
  "count": "2"
}

    The API responds with a JSON similar to the following: 

    
{
    "id": "a86a87d4-cbc2-4d23-8d04-1e282fdfa957",
    "rp_id": "sub_GoqZUVV7RegRVe",
    "authenticationUrl": "https://rzp.io/i/2Yk4OJ5B5h"
}

    Description

    Call this API to buy subscription plan.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/user/pgSubscription

    HTTP Request

    Body Param Description
    pg_subscription_plan_id Plan Id of the pg subscription
    count Number of Drones you want to buy

    Cancel Subscription

       curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/user/pgSubscription/<subscriptionID>"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -X DELETE

      
  {
   "message":"DELETED"
}

    Description

    This API used to cancel the user subscription.

    HTTP Request

    DELETE ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/user/pgSubscription/<subscriptionId>

    HTTP Response

    A response of the above API is message filed with "DELETED".

    { "message":"DELETED" }

    Get User Viewer Minutes Stats

       curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/user/viewerMinutes"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -X GET

    The above API responds with the following JSON

      
{
  quota: 2000,
  used: 1000
}

    Description

    The View Minutes Stats API is called to get the Viewer Minutes stats of the user which include the total quota (in minutes) of viewer minutes that the user has and the number of viewer minutes that have already been used (in minutes) in the user's account

    HTTP Request

    GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/user/viewerMinutes

    HTTP Response

    The response of the API contains a JSON with two fields "quota" (total viewer minutes quota in minutes) and "used" (used viewer minutes in minutes)

    { quota: 2000, used: 1000 }

    Stream Viewer Heartbeat

       curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/viewersHeartbeat/tick"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -X POST

    The above API responds with the following JSON

      
{
    "message": "OK"
}

    Description

    Whenever client is watching AeroStream Live videos at that time above API call after every 2 minutes. Above API updates users viewer minutes quota.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/viewersHeartbeat/tick

    HTTP Response

    The response of the API contains a JSON with message filed with 'OK'

    { "message":"OK" }

    Get Licence Key API

       curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/license"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X POST -D `{
    "publicKey":"Enter your RSA 2048 public key here"
  }`

    A above API produce the following result if you are not enter the valid license key:

    {
    "message": "You are not authorized to view this information"
}

    A above API produce the following result if you enter the valid license key:

    {
    "message": "You are authorized to view this information"
}

    Description

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/license

    HTTP Response

    A above API produce the following result if you are not enter the valid license key

    { "message": "You are not authorized to view this information" }

    A above API produce the following result if you enter the valid license key

    { "message": "You are authorized to view this information" }

    NPNT Flow

    NPNT Flow Generate UUID

      curl "${BASE_URL}/fmr/uuid"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -X GET

    {
  "UUID":"8e199052-e36c-46a4-b558-61fcb9039112"
}

    Description

    A NPNT flow generate UUID API generate UUID and request to GCS for send generated UUID to the server.

    HTTP Request

    GET ${BASE_URL}/fmr/uuid

    HTTP Response

    The above API provide the response like following format.

    { "UUID":"8e199052-e36c-46a4-b558-61fcb9039112" }

    Link User,UUID and Drone API

      curl "${BASE_URL}/fmr/drones"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X PUT -D `{
        "droneID": "drone_id",
        "uuid": "users_UUID",
        "username": "user_name"
        }`

     {
    "droneID": "AV001",
    "UUID": "2ce56d89-2a32-4316-aa31-5184070d594c",
    "username": "scott"
}

    Make sure replacedrone_id, users_UUID, user_name with your drone_id, users_UUID, user_name.

    Description

    The above API used to assign UUID to drone and drone assign to user the link between the UUID, drone and user provide by the above API.

    HTTP Request

    PUT ${BASE_URL}/fmr/drones

    HTTP Response

    The above API provide the following response

    { "droneID": "AV001", "UUID": "2ce56d89-2a32-4316-aa31-5184070d594c", "username": "scott" }

    NPNT Flow Check Drone Ownership API

     curl "${BASE_URL}/checkOwnership/:droneID"
 -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
 -X GET

    Make sure replacedrone_IDwith your drone_ID.

    {
    "ownership": "1"
 }

    Description

    HTTP Request

    GET ${BASE_URL}/checkOwnership/:droneID

    Replace drone_ID with your drone ID.

    HTTP Response

    A above API returns response in following json body format:

    { "ownership": "1" }

  -X POST
  -D '{

    "gcs_title": "AeroGCS",
    "copyright": "PDRL 2021",
    "website": "https://pdrl.in",
    "gcs_splash_screen": "https://test.aeromegh.com/api/hosted/8a9f64fb-d361-459a-ab43-68c3deb0b018.jpg",

    "drone_utility_logo": "https://test.aeromegh.com/api/hosted/8a9f64fb-d361-459a-ab43-68c3deb0b018.jpg"

    "message": "created" 
}

    Activate OEM License

       curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/OEM/activateLicense/1cafc98a-9910-4462-9f1b-ad8162f0fd55
-H 
-X PUT
"body": 
  {
    "member_username": "testpdrl@mailinator.com",
    "installation_id": "02346e48-ab9f-41d3-bd0b-7b5b1af1f818"
  }

     
    A susccessful response with status code 200 :
    {
      "message": "License activated successfully !",
      "access_token": "a134256d-3374-44fe-9861-02d1ec7237f3"
    }

    Description

    This API will be used to activate the OEM license after GCS installation.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/OEM/activateLicense/:license_id

    HTTP Response

    A susccessful request to the above API returns a successful message with status code 200

    { "message": "License activated successfully !" }

    Response codes explanation:

    Code Details
    500 An internal server error has occured.(Datatable related specific message)
    202 Invalid license Id. / License is already activated
    403 Unauthorized attempt to activate license by user invalidUser@gmail.com / Member does not exist !
    400 Request missing parameters
    200 Response shown on the right side.

    Transfer OEM License

       curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/OEM/transferLicense
  -H 
  -X POST
  "body": 
    {
      "license_id": "02346e48-ab9f-41d3-bd0b-7b5b1af1f818"
    }
  
     
      A susccessful response with status code 201 :
      {
        "message": "License transferred successfully."
      }

    Description

    This API will be used to transfer the OEM license for GCS installation.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/OEM/transferLicense

    HTTP Response

    A susccessful request to the above API returns a successful message with status code 201

    { "message": "License transferred successfully." }

    Response codes explanation:

    Code Details
    500 An internal server error has occured.(Datatable related specific message)
    202 Provided license key is invalid./ Provided license key is not activated.
    403 The user has exceeded license transfer limit.
    400 Request missing parameters
    201 License transferred successfully.

    Add new member

       curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/OEM//addMember
  -H  "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -X POST
  "body": 
    {
      "userName": "Test@gmail.com"
      "firstName": "Test"
      "lastName": "OEM"
      "phoneNo": "9999999999"
    }
  
     
      A susccessful response with status code 200 :
      {
        "message": "Member added successfully !"
      }

    Description

    This API will be used to add a new member to manufacturer. It will take the inputs in body as shown on the right.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/OEM/addMember

    HTTP Response

    A susccessful request to the above API returns a successful message with status code 200

    { "message": "Member added successfully !" }

    Response codes explanation:

    Code Details
    500 An internal server error has occured.(Datatable related specific message)
    403 Invalid access token.
    409 Member already exist with given email under this manufacturer
    400 Request missing parameters
    200 Member added successfully !

    Assign OEM Licenses to member

     curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/OEM/assignLicense"
-H  Authorization: Bearer access_token
-X  PUT

"body": 
{
  "member_id": "2346e48-ab9f-41d3-bd0b-7b5b1af1f818",
  "count": 2
}

     
A susccessful response with status code 200 :
{
"message": "2 Licenses assigned to the member successfully. 
            Mail containing license keys has been sent to 
            the member."
}

    Description

    This API will be used to assign the OEM licenses to the member. This api will be used by manufacturer to assign license.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/OEM/assignLicense

    Response codes explanation:

    Code Details
    500 An internal server error has occured.(Datatable related specific message)
    202 You cannot assign license as all licenses are assigned.
    403 Member does not exist under this manufacturer
    400 Request missing parameters
    200 Successful Response

    Register Drone on AeroMegh

      curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/drone/registration"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X POST 
  -D
{
  "droneID": "<droneID>",
  "droneName": "<droneName>",
  "existingDroneToBeReplaced": "<droneID>"
}

    The API responds with a JSON similar to the following: 

    
{
    "message": "Drone has been registered",
    "aerostack": {
      "id": "9002540f-6298-4754-bca0-c83ce215ac9d",
      "user_id": "ebe11010-e493-4f8a-98bf-9b986a7ef694",
      "public_key": "asdasdasd",
      "challenge": null,
      "upstream_topic": "rc8cyk52farns4j9yrocrrakti79k6kxctho6z2nkpnz58dnd5wdrh2y6sfim0ez",
      "downstream_topic": "crl9w41z60dzd5dat7pm5ckbqpiow0r3wsfayg2c0b6skxqw21emc54edlse5axu",
      "api_token": "12b25209-54d0-4c22-83e9-e983c9f71277",
      "session_start": "2021-02-22T10:49:10.693Z",
      "drone_id": "TD786",
      "as_type": 1,
      "created_on": "2021-02-22T10:49:10.466Z",
      "verification_attempt": 1,
      "drone_link_attempt": 1,
      "latest_keep_alive": null
    }
}

    Description

    Call this API to register a new drone under your account. This API takes an optional parameter called existingDroneToBeReplaced. In case the user has reached their drone registration subscription limit, the user may specify an already registered drone in this parameter and the API will replace the same with the new drone ID specified

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/drone/registration

    HTTP Request

    Body Param Description
    droneID The drone ID to be newly registerd under the user's account
    droneName A user friendly name string to identify the drone in AeroMegh and its apps
    existingDroneToBeReplaced* In case the user has reached the drone registration limit, the user can send the ID of a drone that is already registered under the user's account. This specified drone will be replaced with the new drone that is being registered

    * = optional

    HTTP Response

    Case Response Status Code Response Body
    Internal server error 500 {message: "An internal error has occured"}
    Drone ownership check failure for an npnt customer 404 {message: "Drone ownership check failed"}
    Drone registered successfully; Drone was not registered already in aeromegh 201 {message:"Drone has been registered"}
    The user does not have an active subscription to AeroGCS Enterprise plan. 202 {message:"The user is not subscribed to any active plan."}
    The user has reached their drone registration limit. 203 {message:"User has exceeded drone usage limit."}

    Get Streaming Status of One Drone

      curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/drone/stream/<droneID>"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X GET

    The API responds with a JSON similar to the following: 

    
{
    "streamStatus": 0
}

    Description

    Call this API to get the streaming status of a drone. Check whether the drone is associated with an online live stream, a previous unfinished live stream or not associated with any live streams.

    HTTP Request

    GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/drone/stream/<droneID>

    HTTP Request

    URL Params Description
    droneID ID of the drone of which the stream status needs to be queried

    HTTP Response

    Case Response Status Code Response Body
    Internal server error 500 {message: "An internal error has occured"}
    Drone is not registered in user's accoutn 404 {"error": "Drone TD298 not found in your account"}
    Successful query 200 {"streamStatus": 0}

    streamStatus Descriptions

    streamStatus Description
    -1 The drone is being used for a stream and the stream is live as well
    1 The drone was being used for an unfinished stream; the stream is offline
    0 The drone is free and is not bound to any streams currently

    Get Streaming Status of All Drones

      curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/drone/stream"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X GET

    The API responds with a JSON similar to the following: 

    
{
    "drones": [
        {
            "drone_id": "TD297",
            "drone_name": "test_drone_297",
            "userid": "a1ad4014-09dc-4b06-9b43-66255fe01d49",
            "project": null,
            "plan": null,
            "last_keep_alive": null,
            "last_tele_data": null,
            "total_flight_time": {},
            "last_flight_log": null,
            "flight_id": null,
            "stream_key": null,
            "streamStatus": 0
        }
    ]
}

    Description

    This API is called to get the streaming status of all the drones that are registered under the user's aeromegh account

    HTTP Request

    GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/drone/stream

    HTTP Response

    The response gives an array of drones along with their stream statuses in the key "streamStatus"

    Save Last Live Location Of Drone

    curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/drone/liveLocation"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -X POST
  -D '{
    "droneID":"TD786",
    "teleData": {
        "lon":"73.830146999999997",
        "lat":"19.970293000000002",
        "alt":"-6.88e05",
        "vel":"0",
        "dir":"64",
        "bat":"65535",
        "sat":"0",
        "rol":"0.0437218249",
        "pit":"0.0981939584",
        "yaw":"1.11848533",
        "mod":"0",
        "sys":"3"
    }
}'

    Following JSON response is generated with status code 200: json { "message": "OK" }

    Description

    This API is used to save live location of the drone in database.

    HTTP Request

    Request:

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/drone/liveLocation

    Headers:

    { "authorization": "Bearer TOKEN" }

    Body:

    { "droneID":"TD786", "teleData": { "lon":"73.830146999999997", "lat":"19.970293000000002", "alt":"-6.88e05", "vel":"0", "dir":"64", "bat":"65535", "sat":"0", "rol":"0.0437218249", "pit":"0.0981939584", "yaw":"1.11848533", "mod":"0", "sys":"3" } }

    HTTP Response

    The response of above API in the form of json body

    { "message": "OK" }

  -X POST
  -D '{
    "droneID":"TD786",
    "teleData": {
        "lon":"73.830146999999997",
        "lat":"19.970293000000002",
        "alt":"-6.88e05",
        "vel":"0",
        "dir":"64",
        "bat":"65535",
        "sat":"0",
        "rol":"0.0437218249",
        "pit":"0.0981939584",
        "yaw":"1.11848533",
        "mod":"0",
        "sys":"3"
    },
    "flightID": "917fb3e4-7eeb-42fb-8542-ce4847dcce65",
    "key" : "AS_FLIGHT_LOG",
    "aerostakID" : "917fb3e4-7eeb-42fb-8542-ce4847dcce65"
}'

    The API responds with a JSON similar to the following: 

    
{
    "quota": 15600,
    "used": 0
}

    Description

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/RequestADrone/pilot/flight/data

    Headers:

    { "authorization": "Bearer TOKEN" }

    Body:

    { "droneID":"TD786", "teleData": { "lon":"73.830146999999997", "lat":"19.970293000000002", "alt":"-6.88e05", "vel":"0", "dir":"64", "bat":"65535", "sat":"0", "rol":"0.0437218249", "pit":"0.0981939584", "yaw":"1.11848533", "mod":"0", "sys":"3" }, "flightID":"917fb3e4-7eeb-42fb-8542-ce4847dcce65", "key":"AS_FLIGHT_LOG", "aerostackID":"917fb3e4-7eeb-42fb-8542-ce4847dcce65" }

    Get Last Live Location Of Drone

      curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/drone/liveLocation/<droneID>"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X GET

    The API responds with a JSON similar to the following: 

    
{
    "lon": "73.830146999999997",
    "lat": "19.970293000000002",
    "alt": "-6.88e05",
    "vel": "0",
    "dir": "64",
    "bat": "65535",
    "sat": "0",
    "rol": "0.0437218249",
    "pit": "0.0981939584",
    "yaw": "1.11848533",
    "mod": "0",
    "sys": "3",
    "timestamp": "2021-02-26T07:19:04.447Z"
}

    Description

    Call this API to get the last live location of a drone.

    HTTP Request

    Request:

    GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/drone/liveLocation/<droneID>

    Headers:

    { "authorization": "Bearer TOKEN" }

    URL Params Description
    droneID ID of the drone of which the last location needs to be queried

    HTTP Response

    The response gives an object with lat and long

    Add NPNT Customer API

      curl "${BASE_URL}/addCustomer"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X POST-D`{
  "Company Name":"company_name" ,
  "Company CIN": "company_CIN",
  "Company GST Number": company_gst_number
  "DGCA ID":"DGCA_ID",
  "Website":"website",
  "Company Logo":"company_logo",
  "Company Address":"company_address",
  "First Name":"first_name",
  "Last Name":"last_name",
  "Email":"email",
  "Phone Number":"phone_number",
  "password":"password"
   }`

    Make sure to replace company_name,company_CIN,company_gst_number,DGCA_ID,website,company_logo,company_address,first_name,last_name,email,phone_number,password with your customer details.

    The above request returns a response like this:

    {
  "CompanyName": "company_name",
  "CompanyCIN": "company_CIN",
  "CompanyGSTNumber": "company_gst_number",
  "DGCAID": "DGCA_ID",
  "Website": "website",
  "CompanyLogo": "company_logo",
  "CompanyAddress": "company_address",
  "FirstName": "first_name",
  "LastName": "last_name",
  "Email": "email",
  "PhoneNumber": "phone_number",
  "password": "password"
   }

    Description

    Using this API we can add customer details and send all data related to customer on the server using POST method.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/addCustomer

    Replace company_name,company_gst,company_gst_number,DGCA_ID,website,company_logo,company_address,first_name,last_name,email,phone_number,password with your customer details.

    HTTP Response

    A valid request to the Add NPNT Customer API returns the following JSON object in the response body.

    { "Company Name": company_name, "Company CIN": company_CIN, "Company GST Number": company_gst_number, "DGCA ID": DGCA_ID, "Website": website, "Company Logo": company_logo, "Company Address": company_address, "First Name": first_name, "Last Name": last_name, "Email": email, "Phone Number": phone_number, "password": password }

   "password":"password"
   }`

    {

  "DGCAID": "DGCA_ID",
  "Website": "website",

  "CompanyAddress": "company_address",

    Description

    The PUT method is used to request the server to store the included entity-body at a location specified by the edit NPNT customer API . The Edit NPNT Customer API perfoms a edit operation.If the customers wants to change their information, they can change with help of Edit Customer API.

    HTTP Request

    PUT ${BASE_URL}/customer/:organization_ID

    Replace company_name,company_CIN,company_gst_number,DGCA_ID,website,company_logo,company_address,first_name,last_name,email,phone_number,password. with your customer details.

    HTTP Response

    A valid request to the Edit NPNT Customer API returns the following JSON object in the response body

    { "Company Name": company_name, "Company CIN": company_CIN, "Company GST Number": company_gst_number, "DGCA ID": DGCA_ID, "Website": website, "Company Logo": company_logo, "Company Address": company_address, "First Name": first_name, "Last Name": last_name, "Email": email, "Phone Number": phone_number, "password": password }

    Delete NPNT Customer API

     curl "${BASE_URL}/customer/:organization_ID"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X DELETE

    Make sure to replace organization_ID with your organization_ID.

    Descritpion

    The DELETE method is used to request the server to delete a file at a location specified by the delete NPNT Customer API. The Delete NPNT Customer API performs a delete operation it removes all current customers.

    HTTP Request

    DELETE ${BASE_URL}/customer/:organization_ID

    Replace organization_ID with your organization_ID .

    HTTP Response

    A valid request to the Delete NPNT RPAS Model API delete the current customer from server.

    Drone Control Center

    Get Stream Key

      curl "${BASE_URL}/getStreamKey/drone_id"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X GET

    Make sure to replace drone_id with your drone ID

    The above request returns a response like this:

    {
"stream_key": "xjmc1rm1",
"stream_uri": "rtmp://aeromegh.in/LiveApp/{}"
}

    Description

    This API is used to get a stream key for publish video stream of the drone. Along with the stream key, the API also returns a stream_uri which is the URL to which the stream must be published.

    In the stream_uri string, the characters "{}" must be replaced with the stream key given in the response.

    HTTP Request

    GET ${BASE_URL}/getStreamKey/drone_id

    Replace drone_id with your drone ID.

    HTTP Response

    A valid request to this API returns the following JSON object in the response body.

    { "stream_key": "xjmc1rm1", "stream_uri": "rtmp://aeromegh.in/LiveApp/{}" }

    Upload Video To Blob

     curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/Streams/uploadVideo/<flightID>/<streamKey>"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer Token"
  -H "Content-Type: form-data"
  -X POST

    The API responds status 200 with follwing message on successfull video upload.

      {
    "message": "File Uploaded Successfully"
  }

    The API responds status 201 if video not uploaded

      {
    "message": "File not uploaded"
  }

    Description

    The API uploads high quality video to blob server. Maximum video files size is 2 GB. It Needs good internet speed.

    HTTP Request

    API: GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/Streams/uploadVideo/<flightID>/<streamKey>

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <aerostackID>"

    HTTP Response

    Please refer the right hand side of the page for detailed response formats.

    The response of this API will contain message field which shows video is uploaded or not.

    VideoStreaming Heartbeat API

    curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/videoStream/heartbeat/droneid"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -X GET

    Make sure replace droneidwith your droneid.

    {
   "message": "your plan limit is over"
}

    Description

    When the user's videostreaming is start in AeroGcs then the above API call after every 5 minutes and with this API we can get to know about time of videostreaming from when user's started it and if the user's over their limit the above API provide the following response.

    HTTP Request

    GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/videoStream/heartbeat/droneid

    Replace droneid with your droneid.

    HTTP Response

    A valid request to this API returns the following JSON object in the response body.

    `{

    "message": "your plan limit is over" }`

    AeroCapture API's

    Create Task

    curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/aeroCapture/addTask"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -X POST
  --data '{
    "task_name":"lorem",
    "project_id":"9eb4f5e6-62d8-4204-bb16-c6ef6d6919d7",
    "plan_id":"39495b6f-9468-4142-8758-15aceb51a0da",
    "collection_id:"39495b6f-9468-4142-8758-15aceb51a0da",
    "type":["Rusting","Missing Screws"],
    "images":0,
    "anootation_set_id":"39495b6f-9468-4142-8758-15aceb51a0da",
    "accuracy":"low"
  }'

 For detection task : '{
  "task_name":"T2",
  "project_id" : "906514bd-fa47-4a9f-b6d2-1b4e176aadbe",
  "plan_id" : "2923cabb-1211-4371-80b3-e64e9c98b01a",
  "collection_id" : "4681fc0c-0350-47d4-b77e-79457ddebd74",
  "type" : ["fruit_tree"],
  "images" : 5,
  "taskType": "detection",
  "models":[
      {
          "name":"faster_rcnn_inception_v2_pets_car",
          "objects":["fruit_tree"]
      }
  ]
}'

    Make sure replaceaccess_token, task_name,project_id, plan_id,collection_id,type and images with your access_token, name of task, project_id, plan_id, type, and number of images

    {
  "message": "Task created successfully"
}

    Description

    The above API takes the name of the task, list of types, project_id, plan_id,collection_id and image count. If task is training task it will take additional parameters as annotation_set_id and accuracy.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/aeroCapture/addTask

    Replace access_token, task_name, list of types, project_id, plan_id, collection_id and image count with your access_token, name of task

    HTTP Response

    A request of above API provide the following responses:

    Case Status Code Response Body
    Internal server error 500 { message: "Database error has occured"}
    Invalid access token 403 "Invalid access token/key."
    Plan limit 402 { message: `Your plan does not allow to create a task with more than 100 images.` }
    Request missing 400 "Request missing ${parameters}"
    Already exist 409 {message:"Task alredy exist with the same name"}
    Successfull response 200 { message: "Task created successfully"}

    Get Tasks

     curl " GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroCapture/tasks/<project_id>/<plan_id>/<taskName>/<startIndex>/<pageSize>"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"

    A valid request to the above API returns a JSON object in the following format 

    {
    
      "tasks": [
        {
            "user_id": "4a4f24ca-b300-47c9-b5f2-25d6a1ac6346",
            "task_id": "a2032fa5-70ea-4cc5-9396-34992340ef52",
            "date_created": "2021-05-17T08:20:52.675Z",
            "pid": null,
            "images": 0,
            "classes": null,
            "task_name": "abc",
            "status": "idle",
            "plan_id": "39495b6f-9468-4142-8758-15aceb51a0da",
            "project_id": "4a4f24ca-b300-47c9-b5f2-25d6a1ac6346",
            "type": [
                "Rusting",
                "Loose bolts"
            ],
            "plan_name": "Plan01",
            "project_name": "SurveyFieldTest"
        }
    ],
    "count": "1"
    
}

    Description

    The above API provides list of tasks with details. you can search tasks by task name or paginate tasks list through this API. If you want all tasks of user then pass <project_id> and <plan_id> as empty spaces. If you want all task from specific project then pass your <project_id> and pass <plan_id> with empty space And if you want all task from specific plan then you need to pass <project_id> and <plan_id>

    HTTP Request

    API: GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroCapture/tasks/<project_id>/<plan_id>/<taskName>/<startIndex>/<pageSize>

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <bearer_token>"

    HTTP Response

    A valid request to the above API returns a JSON object in the following format

    `{ "tasks": [ { "user_id": "4a4f24ca-b300-47c9-b5f2-25d6a1ac6346", "task_id": "a2032fa5-70ea-4cc5-9396-34992340ef52", "date_created": "2021-05-17T08:20:52.675Z", "pid": null, "images": 0, "classes": null, "task_name": "abc", "status": "idle", "plan_id": "39495b6f-9468-4142-8758-15aceb51a0da", "project_id": "4a4f24ca-b300-47c9-b5f2-25d6a1ac6346", "type": [ "Rusting", "Loose bolts" ], "plan_name": "Plan01", "project_name": "SurveyFieldTest" } ], "count": "1" }`

    Create Project

     curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroCapture/addProject"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X POST -D`{
    "ProjectDetails": {
              "Client_Name": "gdfg",
              "Date and Time": "2020-05-18 16:43:23",
              "FlightCompletedCount": 0,
              "Project_Name": "dfgfd",
              "SoftwareVerison": "1.0"
          }
}`

    A valid request on the API gives this response:

      {
    "message": "OK",
    "project_id": "53d3f3eb-c5d6-4c62-bb5c-9a48c3841f43"
    
  }

    Description

    The create project API is used to add a GCS project under the user's account.

    The API accepts the project's configuration in the request body. The server then creates appropriate files and folders in the user's object storage container and populates them according to the received configuration.
    This project can then be seen in AeroGCS after the next sync cycle.

    HTTP Request

    API: POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroCapture/addProject

    Body: { "ProjectDetails": { "Client_Name": "gdfg", "Date and Time": "2020-05-18 16:43:23", "FlightCompletedCount": 0, "Project_Name": "dfgfd", "SoftwareVerison": "1.0" } }

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <bearer_token>"

    HTTP Response

    A above API returns following response

    { "message": "OK", "project_id": "53d3f3eb-c5d6-4c62-bb5c-9a48c3841f43" }

    Upload image to image collection

     curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroCapture/image/upload/<collection_id>"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -H "Content-Type: form-data"
  -X POST -D`

    A valid request on the API gives this response:

      {
    "message": "Image uploaded successfully"
  }

    Description

    The upload image API used to upload images to aerocapture image collection on container blob.

    The API accepts collection_id, file name and image in base64 format and upload it on aerocapture image collection.

    HTTP Request

    API: POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroCapture/image/upload/<collection_id>

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <bearer_token>"

    append your file in form data

    HTTP Response

    A above API returns following response on successfull file upload.

    Case Response Status Code Response Body
    Internal server error 500 { message: "Database error has occured for table users"}/ Failed to upload image.
    Invalid access token 403 "Invalid access token/key."
    Request missing 400 "Request missing ${parameters}"
    Successfull response 200 Image uploaded susccessfully.

    Create Image Collection

    curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroCapture/addImageCollection"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -X POST
  --body 

 For aeromegh web app:    
    
{
    "project_id":"ccf50584-fa6a-4fab-915b-afe20b6339d0",
    "plan_id":"2a98d014-6809-48c7-8703-ec4b9df2b689",
    "collection_name":"TowerCollection"
}

For GCS desktop app: 

{
  "project_name":"project1",
  "plan_name":"plan1",
  "collection_name":"TowerCollection"
}

    Make sure replaceaccess_token, project_id, plan_id and collection_name with your access_token, project_id, plan_id and collection_name

    {
  
    {
      "message": "Collection created successfully",
      "collection": {
          "id": "6502eec1-f0ab-4088-b211-e2741cb1616f",

      }
  }

    Description

    Given API used to create image collection under the plan. API takes the name of the collection, project_id and plan_id for aeromegh app, for gcs desktop app it takes project_name, plan_name, collection_name.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroCapture/addImageCollection

    Body:
    { "project_id":"ccf50584-fa6a-4fab-915b-afe20b6339d0", "plan_id":"2a98d014-6809-48c7-8703-ec4b9df2b689", "collection_name":"TowerCollection" }

    Replace access_token, project_id, plan_id and collection_name ith your access_token, project_id, plan_id and collection_name

    HTTP Responses

    Code Details
    500 An internal server error has occured.(Datatable related specific message)
    409 Collection name already exist.
    403 Invalid access token.
    400 Request missing parameters.
    200 Result shown on the right side.
    }

  -X POST
  --data '{
    "videoURL":"https://pdrlimage.blob.core.windows.net/container1/DroneStreams/0e23df57-f262-4043-81ce-8006d870d31b/a36i1g5p.mp4?st=2021-08-11T20%3A32%3A20Z&se=2021-08-18T20%3A32%3A20Z&sp=rdl&sv=2018-03-28&sr=c&sig=wj7FxuBeIkvBh%2BKAaAAHM9Sj0%2F7xlufYjiXXI1L7DIA%3D",
    "collectionId":"3d9f8eb7-5b37-4ca6-a032-bd6ff3fae015",
    "fps":1
}'

    Make sure replaceaccess_token, videoURL, collectionId and fps with your access_token, videoURL, collectionId and fps

    {
  "message": "Video imported from aerostream successfully"
}

    Description

    Given API used to import the existing aerostream videos into aerocapture, split into images and store this splitted images under the aerocapture image collection.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroCapture/importVideoFromAeroStream/code>

    Body:
    { "videoURL":"https://pdrlimage.blob.core.windows.net/container1/DroneStreams/0e23df57-f262-4043-81ce-8006d870d31b/a36i1g5p.mp4?st=2021-08-11T20%3A32%3A20Z&se=2021-08-18T20%3A32%3A20Z&sp=rdl&sv=2018-03-28&sr=c&sig=wj7FxuBeIkvBh%2BKAaAAHM9Sj0%2F7xlufYjiXXI1L7DIA%3D", "collectionId":"3d9f8eb7-5b37-4ca6-a032-bd6ff3fae015", "fps":1 }
