                      [ 0.670203685760498, 0.670203685760498],
                      [ 0.670203685760498, 0.670203685760498],
                  ],
                  "percentage": "90.0"
                }
                ],
                "count": 3
            },
            "car": {
                "data": [],
                "count": 0
            }
        }
    }
    
}

    A valid request to the above API returns a JSON object in the following format with status code 200 

    {
    
    "message": "saved"
    
}

    Description

    The above API saves the results of detection performed on an image

    The API takes 3 major properties in its request body. i.e.

    1. task: the task id being executed

    2. image: file name of the image

    3. result: the detection result JSON object

    Below is a sample detection result object

    { "objects": [ "car", "person" ], "detections": { "person": { "data": [ { "poly": [ 0.31104170382022858, 0.47249069809913635, 0.9928195476531982, 0.670203685760498 ], "percentage": "99.0" }, { "poly": [ 0.24013450741767883, 0.6643144488334656, 0.9891364574432373, 0.8799231648445129 ], "percentage": "98.0" }, { "poly": [ 0.1502569615840912, 0.22375090420246124, 1, 0.4686063230037689 ], "percentage": "90.0" } ], "count": 3 }, "car": { "data": [], "count": 0 } } }

    HTTP Request

    API: POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroCapture/detection/results

    Body: Format of the JSON body is give on the right side of this article

    Authorization

    This API does not take any authorization headers. Instead, the API works by comparing the request client's IP address against a list of all the AeroCapture VM nodes which is stored in the server's database.

    HTTP Response

    A valid request to the above API returns a JSON object in the following format with status code 200

    { "message": "saved" }

    Response codes explanation:

    Code Details
    500 The server crashed due to some internal error. The request is OK.
    400 Bad request. The specified image name or collection id does not exist
    403 The client is not an authorized AeroCapture VM node.
    200 Request completed successfully

    Upload detected video file

     curl " POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroCapture/results/video/:taskId"
  -H "Content-Type: Multipart/form-data"

    A valid request to the above API returns a JSON object in the following format with status code 200 

    {
    
    "message": "Video uploaded successfully"
    
}

    Description

    The above API saves the resultant video

    The API takes a file in the form-data body

    1. file: the resultant mp4 file after detection

    Additionally, the API also requires a URL param at the end of the URL i.e.

    1. taskId: The task id of the task to which the detection belongs to

    HTTP Request

    API: POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroCapture/results/video/f261d5b1-731b-40c7-a055-3c59db7cecb1

    Authorization

    This API does not take any authorization headers. Instead, the API works by comparing the request client's IP address against a list of all the AeroCapture VM nodes which is stored in the server's database.

    HTTP Response

    A valid request to the above API returns a JSON object in the following format with status code 200

    { "message": "Video uploaded successfully" }

    Response codes explanation:

    Code Details
    500 The server crashed due to some internal error. The request is OK.
    404 Invalid taskId. The task id does not exist
    403 The client is not an authorized AeroCapture VM node.
    200 Request completed successfully

    Save Video Detection Results

     curl " POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroCapture/detection/video/results"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"

    Below is a sample request body 

    {
    
    "task": "51e298af-9dc7-4afd-91c3-7ba724b7f9ea",
    "result": {
      "timestamp": "1626214227",
      "file_name": "output-cracks.mp4",
      "fps": "",
      "resolution": "480"
    }
    
}

    A valid request to the above API returns a JSON object in the following format with status code 200 

    {
    
    "message": "saved"
    
}

    Description

    The above API saves the results of detection performed on a video

    The API takes 2 major properties in its request body. i.e.

    1. task: the task id being executed

    2. result: the detection result JSON object

    Below is a sample detection result object

    { "timestamp": "1626214227", "file_name": "output-cracks.mp4", "fps": "", "resolution": "480" }

    HTTP Request

    API: POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroCapture/detection/video/results

    Body: Format of the JSON body is give on the right side of this article

    Authorization

    This API does not take any authorization headers. Instead, the API works by comparing the request client's IP address against a list of all the AeroCapture VM nodes which is stored in the server's database.

    HTTP Response

    A valid request to the above API returns a JSON object in the following format with status code 200

    { "message": "saved" }

    Response codes explanation:

    Code Details
    500 The server crashed due to some internal error. The request is OK.
    404 Invalid task. The specified task id does not exist
    403 The client is not an authorized AeroCapture VM node.
    200 Request completed successfully

    Add new Annotation Set

    }

    {

  message : "Annotation set added successfully."

}

    Description

    This API will be called when a user will create an annotation under an existing image set. This API will take inputs in request body - image_collection_id, annotation_set_name, classes, plan_id and after validation it will create the annotation set.

    { message : "Annotation set added successfully." }

    Response codes explanation:

    Code Details
    500 An internal server error has occured.
    403 Invalid access token.
    400 Request missing parameters/ Authorization mode must be bearer.
    409 There is already an annotation set with the same name.
    201 Request completed successfully

  --data 
    {
      "fileName" : "image1",
      "annotation_set_id" : "02c49077-d2ea-400b-9956-f02b54a3d8cd",
      "image_collection_id" : "ce2db60b-d55e-49ef-b546-484154a62c6e",
      "image_data" : {
      "imageName" : "abc.jpeg",
        "annotationData" :[
        {
          "className": "tree",
          "shape": "rectangle",
          "x_point": [
              48.03921568627451,
              22.549019607843142
          ],
          "y_points": [
              38.72549019607843,
              32.843137254901954
          ]
        }
      ]
    } 
  }
}

    Make sure replaceaccess_token, taskName with your access_token, name of task

    {
  "message": "Annotation saved successfully."
  }"

    Description

    The above API takes the name of the existing ML task and fileName without extension. When the API is called, the server creates respective file for the ML Annotation on the server under the given task folder.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/saveMLAnnotation

    Body:
    { { "fileName" : "image1", "annotation_set_id" : "02c49077-d2ea-400b-9956-f02b54a3d8cd", "image_collection_id" : "ce2db60b-d55e-49ef-b546-484154a62c6e", "image_data" : { "imageName" : "abc.jpeg", "annotationData" :[ { "className": "tree", "shape": "rectangle", "x_point": [ 48.03921568627451, 22.549019607843142 ], "y_points": [ 38.72549019607843, 32.843137254901954 ] } ] } } }

    Replace access_token with your access_token

    HTTP Response

    Response Code Message
    200 Annotation saved successfully.
    400 Bad Request -- Your request is missing some required fields/paramters
    403 Forbidden -- Your access token invalid. / Authorization type must be bearer.
    500 An internal server error has occured./ Error while creating file on blob.

    AeroStack Authentication APIs 🔑

    Register a new AeroStack for a user's account

     curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/register"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer user_access_token"

    If the user has a sub available for registering a new aerostack, a new aerostack will be registered and the following response will be received with status code: 201

      {
    "id": "d8e7a5ea-7ff4-4fc4-b861-3a4f0ae690b6",
    "user_id": "4a4f24ca-b300-47c9-b5f2-25d6a1ac6346",
    "username": "curtis.howard@mailinator.com",
    "license": "LBXihoEwjlWcqTUo5w0H06/WHtDihx/F0clI/PF3ENcnSdZOu6M+Hs7e6/3iv+7ZIOwgMs6YR5mlgm7nGojDg8CMao3QtjhUIgK6HH8HXUG0BTnsIWLYJ6BQ9yuPnwf/wn5muRDlDZtmde3QEsLVSgfudTKg57ny5+o1GfxicCixov4fr4kRprVe0Jgdzq7sg0GNFjS8+utRLWJaBK6eRdvsJpmYRhwUxqATt9Tq6+PrHCAhvS2lPlPgJlV4RflP/4HvzdmjtRDrCko7sQw7iGhi/yXaI0k1uIVtmTJUrMGhs+j0v/gS0ULy/G6zbGenNMT88pcJQfk1qn8CGIaE2w=="
  }

    If the user does not have a sub available for registering a new AeroStack, then the following response will be received with status code: 403

      {
    "message": "You don't have any AeroStack subs. Please obtain/purchase one."
  }

    Description

    This API is used on behalf of an AeroMegh user to register a new AeroStack instance.

    For registering a new AeroStack instance, the user must have at least one AeroStack registration sub available.

    If the user has a registration sub available then a new AeroStack is created in the system against that user and a license is generated and returned in the API response. Each AeroStack license is created by using the AeroStack instance's ID and the user ID of the user who created the instance.

    HTTP Request

    API: GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/register

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <user_bearer_token>"

    HTTP Response

    Please refer the right hand side of the page for detailed response formats.

    Response generated by a successful API call contains the ID of the new AeroStack, the user ID and username of the requesting user and the license of the AeroStack instance.

    Verify an AeroStack Registration

     curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/verify"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer aerostackID"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X POST -d '{
      "license": "LBXihoEwjlWcqTUo5w0H06/WHtDihx/F0clI/PF3ENcnSdZOu6M+Hs7e6/3iv+7ZIOwgMs6YR5mlgm7nGojDg8CMao3QtjhUIgK6HH8HXUG0BTnsIWLYJ6BQ9yuPnwf/wn5muRDlDZtmde3QEsLVSgfudTKg57ny5+o1GfxicCixov4fr4kRprVe0Jgdzq7sg0GNFjS8+utRLWJaBK6eRdvsJpmYRhwUxqATt9Tq6+PrHCAhvS2lPlPgJlV4RflP/4HvzdmjtRDrCko7sQw7iGhi/yXaI0k1uIVtmTJUrMGhs+j0v/gS0ULy/G6zbGenNMT88pcJQfk1qn8CGIaE2w==",
      "publicKey": "-----BEGIN PUBLIC KEY-----MIIBIjANBgkqhkiG9w0BAQEFAAOCAQ8AMIIBCgKCAQEAheLDxCWV9PE++uygjd3PlZlsdiuP6QlPWTbgfiBVuOwv4Xi00oawlrBkWAG4yZTbNPakEaYpMbxM7vaVR3n631PSnQtwMZaOXVy63gFVyGldim6BiyUQPeCAMEFs5aND7QKWG4/RwgnPaGfoixYsUjfEvaLvvoH3rAVIk0WIZhRRt7EkOC8UiLI7fA0WCHXH43y5FnYsLqMWER3JaXkQCBdnxrtNKEXfk1+of3cSatu2wCwANtCJC1IOJ1qbEkdNaA5IAU1Aog5F1LnS9pa1lmpprtMVuo2eixCDSCvRm4WZk57dfQmkGhrHpLhJ5OEnLT8USsMWPtvgeQfPzzy8/QIDAQAB-----END PUBLIC KEY-----"
  }'

    If the license sent in the request is verified as valid, then the public key attached in the request will be stored in the system and the following response will be generated with the status code: 200

      {
      "message": "OK"
  }

    If the license verification fails, the following response is generated with a status code: 403

      {
      "message": "License verification failed."
  }

    Description

    This API is called by an AeroStack instance to verify its registration in the system by sending its license.

    Along with the license, the AeroStack instance also sends its RSA 2048 public key. If the license is verified as valid, the sent public key will be stored in the system and used in further communication.

    HTTP Request

    API: POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/verify

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <aerostackID>"

    HTTP Response

    Please refer the right hand side of the page for detailed response formats.

    The response of this API simply returns the verification result of the AeroStack license sent in the request.

    Request an AeroStack Login

     curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/loginRequest"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer aerostackID"

    The API sends a challenge to the requesting AeroStack instance in the following format with the status code: 200

      {
    "challenge": "eV76dNJsWr7OLfkK55NpyMp+Jl7ufZkcxQY6pBgULRpHYUAmZV5pGUnIBWB7ozk7wK5Wl/m5A/0A6W5Ww8f1WpkRt5y3MQ3lHdiRmbhWuKKkCZKdYNwe2ksDTXQChc+Wwj+iCxlOuNFL+HtJ3D4cG5Hjee7fZrlAI9GPniFK+wZLnxNckM5pyI2Vzbgf1zwRBqnVba0KfcM1LWKypolKFNyGtJOkTcQDaK9R/+SHZK6RC6qJCiTuUfM/I6UTwr1ziJWItdvWckJjkpuQcS9fRthUKtdYEe81+PPaafD8kAPNmiycxVubB+S1fTiFf6C3TM0r8iSgEOqR6Wdjek0BFg=="
  }

    Description

    This API is called by an AeroStack instance to request a new login challenge. Upon verification of the response of this challenge, a new login session will be created which will expire in 24 hours.

    HTTP Request

    API: GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/loginRequest

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <aerostackID>"

    HTTP Response

    Please refer the right hand side of the page for detailed response formats.

    The response of this API will contain a login challenge in the body which must be solved by the AeroStack instance and the reponse must be sent back on login verification API.

    The challenge itself is a string which is encrypted using the public key of the AeroStack instance stored in the system during registration verification process.

    Verify AeroStack Login

     curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/loginVerify"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer aerostackID"
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  -X POST -d '{
      "response": "b21dea30-4696-44ac-ba81-68b468b2f4c3"
  }'

    If the login verification fails, following response is generated with the status code: 403

      {
      "message": "Login verification failed"
  }

    If the login verification is successful, a response in the following format is generated with the status code: 200

      {
      "upstream_topic": "231qvwdmfz5ci9rj7y7vb7ah6eldxicsaqb7whrxw27797bgoo89t22f49609e93",
      "downstream_topic": "20trg6c5tq6fsunjuhavndmwxlb4qz1xptfh6mumu3qm08cgz9fjwkl3cnygr8kk",
      "apiToken": "14073615-05c3-4e2f-8b6c-a30aaaa498d2",
      "validTill": "Sat, 25 Jul 2020 11:13:21 GMT"
  }

    Description

    This API is called by an AeroStack instance to submit the repsonse of login challenge for verification. Upon verification of the response, a new login session will be created which will expire in 24 hours and the Kafka topics and api token generated for the session will be returned.

    HTTP Request

    API: POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/loginVerify

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <aerostackID>"

    HTTP Response

    Please refer the right hand side of the page for detailed response formats.

    If a valid response message is sent in the request of this API, the system will create a new AeroStack login instance and will generate and send the following things in the response,
    1. Upstream Kafka Topic
    2. Downstream Kafka Topic
    3. API Bearer Token
    4. Until what timestamp is this session valid

    Flights

    Request a Flight ID

     curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/requestFlightID?projectName=dfgfd&planName=dfgdfg&droneID=TD23&teamId=df76de65-27dd-46ad-9b6b-ce07f56928e3"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"

    The API sends a new flight id in the response with the status code: 201

    
        {
            "flightID": "fac442e3-8608-4846-84d0-b6cc98a2849e",
            "streamKey": "usyfkyts"
        }

    Description

    This API is called by an AeroStack or AeroGCS instance to request a new flight ID just before taking off. The API requires the requesting entity to send the project name, plan name, drone id of the drone which is going to be used for the flight, team id and the user's access token.

    The API generates a new flight record in the system and maps all the received data to the new flight. After doing so, the API returns the flight ID of the newly generated flight.

    HTTP Request

    API: GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/requestFlightID?projectName=dfgfd&planName=dfgdfg&droneID=TD23&teamId=df76de65-27dd-46ad-9b6b-ce07f56928e3"

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <bearer_token>"

    HTTP Response

    Error Code Meaning
    201 { "flightID": "fac442e3-8608-4846-84d0-b6cc98a2849e", "streamKey": "usyfkyts" }
    400 Bad Request -- Your request is missing some required fields/paramters
    403 Invalid access token.
    500 An internal server error has occured.

    The API generates a new flight for the given data and returns the ID of the flight in the response.

    This API must be called right before the drone is taking off.

    End a flight

     curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/endFlight?flightID=d544f7cb-567e-462a-9410-735b95a11423&teamId=c47d4946-e046-46a8-91c9-bf026dd79219"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"

    The API sends in response the following JSON body with a status code: 200

      {
      "message": "OK"
  }

    Description

    This API is called by an AeroStack or AeroGCS instance to mark the end of a drone flight. The API takes in the flight ID and the teamId given at the start of the flight and simply marks the timestamp of the end of the flight.

    HTTP Request

    API: GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/endFlight?flightID=d544f7cb-567e-462a-9410-735b95a11423&teamId=c47d4946-e046-46a8-91c9-bf026dd79219

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <access_token>"

    HTTP Response

    Please refer the right hand side of the page for detailed response formats.

    The API responds with a simple JSON body containing the message OK

    This API must be called right the drone has landed.

    Add offline flight logs

    Add offline flight logs

       curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/addOfflineLogs"
-H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
-H "projectName : test"
-H "planName: test"
-H "aerostackid: b1a34f98-4b22-4051-9407-d4ef64f318d5"
-H "flightid: a2a34f98-4b22-4051-9407-d4ef64f318d5"
-H "teamid: a2a34f98-4b22-4051-9407-d4ef64f318d5"
-H "droneid: P000010032001C3037511037323939"
-X POST

    The above API responds with the following JSON

      
{
"message": "Logs added"
}

    Description

    This API is used to update the offline flight logs of a flight.This API also requires the csv file of the flight logs. Make sure to add the file along side with this API call. It reads the log data from the file and updates the database accordingly.

    HTTP Request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/addOfflineLogs

    HTTP Response

    Error Code Meaning
    200 { message : Logs added. }
    400 Bad Request -- Your request is missing some required fields/paramters
    403 Invalid access token.
    500 An internal server error has occured.

    Map/Link Drone to AeroStack

    import http.client

conn = http.client.HTTPConnection("${BASE_URL}")

payload = "{\n\t\"aerostackID\": \"AS123\",\n\t\"droneID\": \"TD26\"\n}"

headers = {
    'content-type': "application/json",
    'authorization': "Bearer b2a4e7dd-0224-4161-a33e-8c67a7ba07dc"
    }

conn.request("POST", "/AeroMegh/AeroStack/mapDrone", payload, headers)

res = conn.getresponse()
data = res.read()

print(data.decode("utf-8"))

    var data = JSON.stringify({
  "aerostackID": "AS123",
  "droneID": "TD26"
});

var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
xhr.withCredentials = true;

xhr.addEventListener("readystatechange", function () {
  if (this.readyState === this.DONE) {
    console.log(this.responseText);
  }
});

xhr.open("POST", "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/mapDrone");
xhr.setRequestHeader("content-type", "application/json");
xhr.setRequestHeader("authorization", "Bearer b2a4e7dd-0224-4161-a33e-8c67a7ba07dc");

xhr.send(data);

    curl --request POST \
 --url ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/mapDrone \
 --header 'authorization: Bearer b2a4e7dd-0224-4161-a33e-8c67a7ba07dc' \
 --header 'content-type: application/json' \
 --data '{
 "aerostackID": "AS123",
 "droneID": "TD26"
}'

    The API sends in response the following JSON body with a status code: 200

      {
    "message": "OK"
  }

    Description

    This API is used to link a drone to an aerostack instance. The drone and aerostack being sent in the request should be registered under the user's account in AeroMegh.

    HTTP Request

    API: POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/getDronesStatus

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <access_token>"

    Body:
    { "aerostackID": "AS123", "droneID": "TD26" }

    HTTP Response

    Please refer the right hand side of the page for detailed response formats.

    The API responds with a simple OK message with the standard HTTP status code 200.

    Send Flight Command

    

    

    curl --request GET 
 --url ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/sendFlightCommand?droneID=drone_id&command=cmd  
 --header 'authorization: Bearer b2a4e7dd-0224-4161-a33e-8c67a7ba07dc' 
 --header 'content-type: application/json'

    The API sends in response the following JSON body with a status code: 200

      {
    "message": "OK"
  }

    Description

    The above API used to send command to the Aerostack module which is link with drone_id.

    HTTP Request

    API: GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/sendFlightCommand?droneID=drone_id&command=cmd

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <access_token>"

    Replace drone_id and cmd with the your drone_id and cmd.

    HTTP Response

    A valid request to the Social Distancing API returns a JSON response in the following format

    `{

    "message": "OK"

    } `

    Flight Scheduling

    Schedule Flight / Create New Flight Schedule

    import http.client

conn = http.client.HTTPConnection("${BASE_URL}")

payload = "{\n    \"droneID\": \"TD26\", \n    \"projectName\": \"Mumbai111\", \n    \"planName\": \"Day111\", \n    \"repeat\": \"0\", \n    \"dow\": \"[1, 2, 3, 4, 5]\", \n    \"dom\": \"17\", \n    \"date_of_flight\": \"2020-08-20\", \n    \"time_of_flight\": \"13:05:00\"\n}"

headers = {
    'content-type': "application/json",
    'authorization': "Bearer b2a4e7dd-0224-4161-a33e-8c67a7ba07dc"
    }

conn.request("POST", "/AeroMegh/AeroStack/createFlightSchedule", payload, headers)

res = conn.getresponse()
data = res.read()

print(data.decode("utf-8"))

    var data = JSON.stringify({
  "droneID": "TD26",
  "projectName": "Mumbai111",
  "planName": "Day111",
  "repeat": "0",
  "dow": "[1, 2, 3, 4, 5]",
  "dom": "17",
  "date_of_flight": "2020-08-20",
  "time_of_flight": "13:05:00"
});

var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
xhr.withCredentials = true;

xhr.addEventListener("readystatechange", function () {
  if (this.readyState === this.DONE) {
    console.log(this.responseText);
  }
});

xhr.open("POST", "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/createFlightSchedule");
xhr.setRequestHeader("content-type", "application/json");
xhr.setRequestHeader("authorization", "Bearer b2a4e7dd-0224-4161-a33e-8c67a7ba07dc");

xhr.send(data);

    curl --request POST \
  --url ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/createFlightSchedule \
  --header 'authorization: Bearer b2a4e7dd-0224-4161-a33e-8c67a7ba07dc' \
  --header 'content-type: application/json' \
  --data '{
    "droneID": "TD26",
    "projectName": "Mumbai111",
    "planName": "Day111",
    "repeat": "0",
    "dow": "[1, 2, 3, 4, 5]",
    "dom": "20",  
    "moy": "08",  
    "date_of_flight": "2020-08-20",
    "time_of_flight": "13:05:00"
}'

    The API sends in response the following JSON body with a status code: 200

      {
    "message": "OK"
  }

    Description

    This API is used to create a new flight schedule in the system. Schedules could be repeating or non repeating. Repeating flight schedules have the following modes:
    1. Daily: The flight will repeat everyday at the specified time
    2. Weekly: The flight will repeat on the specified time on the specified day(s) of each week
    3. Monthly: The flight will repeat on the specified time of the specified day of each month
    4. Yearly: The flight will repeat on the specified time of the specified date of each year

    HTTP Request

    API: POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroStack/createFlightSchedule

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <access_token>"

    Body: { "droneID": "TD26", "projectName": "Mumbai111", "planName": "Day111", "repeat": "0", "dow": "[1, 2, 3, 4, 5]", "dom": "20", "moy": "08", "date_of_flight": "2020-08-20", "time_of_flight": "13:05:00" }

    Body Key Description
    droneID Drone ID of the drone which is to be used for the flight
    projectName The name of the project in which the plan to be followed exists
    planName The name of the plan that is to be followed
    repeat Represents the repeat mode of the schedule. Repeat modes are explained below
    dow For weekly flights, array containing the days of week on which the flight must take place. 0=Sunday, 1=Monday etc. Must be in format: [2, 5, 6]
    dom For monthly and yearly flights, the day of each month on which the flight must take place
    moy For yearly flights, the month on which the flight must take place
    date_of_flight For non repeating flights, the exact date on which the flight must take place
    time_of_flight The exact time at which the flight must take place
    Repeat Mode Code Description
    0 Do not repeat. Fly once.
    1 Repeat daily
    2 Repeat weekly
    3 Repeat monthly
    4 Repeat yearly

    HTTP Response

    Please refer the right hand side of the page for detailed response formats.

    The API simply responds with an OK message.

    User Wallet

    Download Postman Collection

    Check your wallet balance

    import http.client

conn = http.client.HTTPConnection("${BASE_URL}")

headers = {
    'content-type': "application/json",
    'authorization': "Bearer TOKEN"
    }

conn.request("GET", "/AeroMegh/users/wallet/balance", headers)

res = conn.getresponse()
data = res.read()

print(data.decode("utf-8"))

    var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
xhr.withCredentials = true;

xhr.addEventListener("readystatechange", function () {
  if (this.readyState === this.DONE) {
    console.log(this.responseText);
  }
});

xhr.open("GET", "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/users/wallet/balance");
xhr.setRequestHeader("content-type", "application/json");
xhr.setRequestHeader("authorization", "Bearer TOKEN");

xhr.send(data);

    curl --request GET \
  --url ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/users/wallet/balance \
  --header 'authorization: Bearer TOKEN' \
  --header 'content-type: application/json' \

    The API sends in response the following JSON body with a status code: 200

      {
    "balance": 0,
    "currency": "INR"
  }

    Description

    A user can call this API and get their available wallet balance.

    HTTP Request

    API: GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/users/wallet/balance

    Headers: "authorization": "Bearer <access_token>"

    HTTP Response

    The API sends in response a JSON containing the balance remaining in the user's wallet along with the currency in which the balance is represented.

    Please refer the right hand side of the page for detailed response formats.

    User services

    Download Postman Collection

    Get AeroMegh Services Subscribed by User API

    curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/subbedServices"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -X GET

    Description

    This API can be called by or on behalf of a user to request the list of all the AeroMegh services that are activated on the user's AeroMegh account.

    HTTP Request

    GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/subbedServices

    HTTP Response

    { "services": [ { "id": "123", "title": "Remote Mission Planning" }, { "id": "234", "title": "NPNT Services" } ] }

    Self-activate a service

    curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/users/services/activate"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -X POST
  -D '
  {
    "services": [
      {
        "serviceID": "123",
        "invoiceID": "re_123",
        "serviceActivationCallbackOptions": {
          "radUserType": 1
        }
      }
    ]
  }
  '

    When activation and invoice verification is successful, following JSON response is generated with status code 200: 

     {
  "message": "OK"
 }

    When activation and invoice verification fails, following JSON response is generated with status code 403: 

     {
  "message": "Invoices verification failed"
 }

    Description

    This API allows user to activate an AeroMegh service on their AeroMegh account. There are 2 types of AeroMegh services:

    1. Paid
    2. Free-To-Activate

    The Paid Services require user to present a invoice ID along with the service to be activated. The invoice ID must be of an invoice that was generated during the purchase of a product which includes access to the AeroMegh service which the user wishes to activate

    For the free-to-activate services, invoiceID field is ignored and is therefore optional.

    HTTP Request

    Request:

    GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/subbedServices

    Headers:

    { "authorization": "Bearer TOKEN" }

    HTTP Response

    The API responds with a simple JSON containing a property "message" which either reads "OK" in case the invoice verification and service activation process is done successfully or returns a suitable error.

    For detailed format of the response format, refer to the right side pane.

    Create request-a-drone service request

    curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/RequestADrone/requester/requests"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -X POST
  -D '
  {
    "title": "test1",
    "description": "this is a test request",
    "slotID": "5b7978fa-8ead-465c-992c-dc0df6909c90",
    "location": {
      "lat": 12.1352354,
      "lon": 79.3454262
    },
    "address": "ithech",
    "paymentMethod": 1
  }
  '

    When service creation is successful, following JSON response is generated with status code 200: 

     {
    "message": "CREATED",
    "razorPayOrderID": "ord_4v6v34563"
  }

    Description

    This API allows the user of the request-a-drone AeroMegh service to create a new service request which can be accepted by the pilots and fulfilled.

    HTTP Request

    Request:

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/RequestADrone/requester/requests

    Headers:

    { "authorization": "Bearer TOKEN" }

    Body:

    { "title": "test1", "description": "this is a test request", "slotID": "5b7978fa-8ead-465c-992c-dc0df6909c90", "location": { "lat": 12.1352354, "lon": 79.3454262 }, "address": "ithech", "paymentMethod": 1 }

    Payment methods:

    method code
    pay 0
    wallet 1

    HTTP Response

    The API responds with a simple JSON containing one property "message" which reads "CREATED" and another property "razorPayOrderID". The order ID is not returned when the payment method is set to wallet.

    For detailed format of the response format, refer to the right side pane.

    Settle a payment

    curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/payments/settlePayment"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer access_token"
  -X POST
  -D '{
    "razorPayPaymentID": "pay_Fx4ENWeJytc6x5",
    "razorPaySignature": "e2a4939bd17cb970e5529b9dc8dd7147e85a637cfe8d4ff9c0a24f2d703ed7d5",
    "razorPayOrderID": "ord_3kfuiu9eh2hefh"
  }'

    Following JSON response is generated with status code 200: json { "message": "Settled" }

    Description

    This API is used to settle an open payment. The payment ID or the razorPayOrderID must be sent in the request along with the payment ID and the received signature. Once the signature is verified, the payment is marked as settled in the DB.

    HTTP Request

    Request:

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/payments/settlePayment

    Headers:

    { "authorization": "Bearer TOKEN" }

    Body:

    { "razorPayPaymentID": "pay_Fx4ENWeJytc6x5", "razorPaySignature": "e2a4939bd17cb970e5529b9dc8dd7147e85a637cfe8d4ff9c0a24f2d703ed7d5", "razorPayOrderID": "ord_3kfuiu9eh2hefh" }

    HTTP Response

    The API responds with a JSON containing a "settled" message.

    For detailed format of the response format, refer to the right side pane.

    AeroStream Pilot APIs

    AeroStream Pilot Check Broken Stream

    curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/RequestADrone/pilot/brokenStream/<droneID>"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer TOKEN"
  -X GET

    The API responds with a status code 200 and a JSON response similar to the following, flightID, and streamKey: 

    
{
    "status": 0
}

    Description

    The API is used by the AeroStream Pilot to check if there is an incomplete or unfinished stream that was done from a particular drone. If there was any such stream, the pilot has the option to either continue that stream, end that stream and start a new one, or wait for the stream to get over in case media is still being live streamed on that stream.

    The API responds with a "status" integer. The values of this "status" integer are explained in the HTTP Response section of this API below.

    GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/RequestADrone/pilot/brokenStream/:droneID

    Headers:

    { "authorization": "Bearer TOKEN" }

    HTTP Response

    The API responds with a JSON body with a single key "status". This integer represents the status of stream on the queried drone. The status values are explained below:

    status Description
    0 No unfinished streams. Safe to start new one
    1 An unfinished stream found and media is not being streamed. User may continue the stream or finish it and start a new one.
    -1 An unfinished stream found and media is being streamed. The stream must be stopped first.

    AeroStream Pilot Start Request

    curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/RequestADrone/pilot/startRequest"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer TOKEN"
  -X POST
  -D '{
      "requestID": "<requestID>",
      "droneID": "<droneID>",
      "teamID": "<teamID>",
      "continuePreviousIfPresent": true
    }'

    The API responds with a status code 200 and a JSON response similar to the following containing a message ("OK"), flightID, and streamKey: 

    
{
    "message": "OK",
    "flightID": "2e150edd-3407-43ed-b871-2c58b03c7386",
    "streamKey": "5qwd3392"
}

    Description

    The API is used by the AeroStream Pilot to start a particular flight request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/RequestADrone/pilot/startRequest

    Headers:

    { "authorization": "Bearer TOKEN" }

    Body

    {
    "requestID": "<requestID>",
    "droneID": "<droneID>",
    "teamID": "<teamID>",
    "continuePreviousIfPresent": true,
    }

    Request param Description
    requestID ID of the request to start
    droneID The ID of the drone being used for the flight
    teamID The ID of the team user currently active in
    continuePreviousIfPresent boolean; whether to continue any past unfinished streams (true) or finish any past unfinished streams if present and start new (false)
    <

    HTTP Response

    Error Code Meaning
    200 { "message": "OK", "flightID": "2e150edd-3407-43ed-b871-2c58b03c7386", "streamKey": "5qwd3392" }
    400 Bad Request -- Your request is missing some required fields/paramters
    403 Invalid access token.
    500 An internal server error has occured.

    AeroStream Pilot End Request

    curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/RequestADrone/pilot/endRequest"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer TOKEN"
  -X POST
  -D '{
      "requestID": "<requestID>",
      "flightID": "<flightID>"
    }'

    The API responds with a status code 200 and a JSON response similar to the following containing a message ("OK"): 

    
{
    "message": "OK"
}

    Description

    The API is used by the AeroStream Pilot to end a particular flight request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/RequestADrone/pilot/endRequest

    Headers:

    { "authorization": "Bearer TOKEN" }

    Body

    { "requestID": "<requestID>", "flightID": "<flightID>" }

    Request param Description
    requestID ID of the request to end
    flightID the flightID received when starting the AeroStream flight request

    HTTP Response

    The response body returns an "OK" message.

    Headers:

    Firmware Management

    Get All Firmwares

    curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/NPNT/Manufacturer/firmwares/firmware"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer TOKEN"
  -X GET

    The API responds with a status code 200 and a JSON response similar to the following, flightID, and streamKey: 

    
{
    "status": 0
}

    Description

    The API is used by the AeroStream Pilot to check if there is an incomplete or unfinished stream that was done from a particular drone. If there was any such stream, the pilot has the option to either continue that stream, end that stream and start a new one, or wait for the stream to get over in case media is still being live streamed on that stream.

    The API responds with a "status" integer. The values of this "status" integer are explained in the HTTP Response section of this API below.

    GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/RequestADrone/pilot/brokenStream/:droneID

    Headers:

    { "authorization": "Bearer TOKEN" }

    HTTP Response

    The API responds with a JSON body with a single key "status". This integer represents the status of stream on the queried drone. The status values are explained below:

    status Description
    0 No unfinished streams. Safe to start new one
    1 An unfinished stream found and media is not being streamed. User may continue the stream or finish it and start a new one.
    -1 An unfinished stream found and media is being streamed. The stream must be stopped first.

    AeroStream Pilot Start Request

    curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/RequestADrone/pilot/startRequest"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer TOKEN"
  -X POST
  -D '{
      "requestID": "<requestID>",
      "droneID": "<droneID>",
      "continuePreviousIfPresent": true
    }'

    The API responds with a status code 200 and a JSON response similar to the following containing a message ("OK"), flightID, and streamKey: 

    
{
    "message": "OK",
    "flightID": "2e150edd-3407-43ed-b871-2c58b03c7386",
    "streamKey": "5qwd3392"
}

    Description

    The API is used by the AeroStream Pilot to start a particular flight request

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/RequestADrone/pilot/startRequest

    Headers:

    { "authorization": "Bearer TOKEN" }

    Body

    { "requestID": "<requestID>", "droneID": "<droneID>", "continuePreviousIfPresent": true, }

    Request param Description
    requestID ID of the request to start
    droneID The ID of the drone being used for the flight
    continuePreviousIfPresent boolean; whether to continue any past unfinished streams (true) or finish any past unfinished streams if present and start new (false)

    HTTP Response

    The response body returns an "OK" message, a flightID and a streamKey. The streamKey must be used to publish flight stream, and the flightID must be sent in the next API i.e. /endRequest API to end this request

    AeroGCS Session Management

    Postman Collection Export

    Get new session

    curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroGCS/createNewGCSSession"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer TOKEN"
  -X POST
  -D '{
      "droneID": "P123"
    }'

    The API responds with a JSON similar to the following with status code 200: 

    {
    "upstream_topic": "b2rq24f2jxl39u22f6ihh5qfvg6kkq120k4fljjyr1zmpbcmaubiamxigjhwvrms",
    "downstream_topic": "owkp30isv8nbdut9fhaiqd8t6dbi6c9m6ybixxz9afpv5oajomgo93a33zr9zz6s",
    "streamKey": "0gvjuhvw",
    "validTill": "Wed, 18 Nov 2020 08:38:14 GMT"
}

    Description

    This API creates a new session internally for an AeroGCS instance and returns upstream topic, downstream topic, stream key and the session expiration timestamp associated with the newly created session.

    HTTP Request

    Request:

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/AeroGCS/createNewGCSSession

    Headers:

    { "authorization": "Bearer TOKEN" }

    Body

    In body, send the droneID which is being used in the AeroGCS currently. This drone must already be registered under the user's account. Otherwise this API will fail.

    { "droneID": "P123" }

    HTTP Response

    The API responds with a JSON containing the upstream, downstream kafka topics for the session and the video stream key & session expiration timestamp

  -X GET

    The API responds with a JSON similar to the following with status code 200: 

    {

}

    Description

    This API initiates a new transaction for Aadhaar KYC customer verification. The API responds with a captcha code image to be shown to the user and have the code shown in the image entered by the user along with their aadhaar number.

    HTTP Request

    Request:

    GET ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/aadhaar/startRequest

    Headers:

    { "authorization": "Bearer TOKEN" }

    HTTP Response

    The API response contains a 10 digit transID string which is the ID assigned to each transaction to uniquely identify each transaction. This ID must be sent again in the subsequent 2 APIs request body.

    The API response also contains a captchaCode key which contains the base64 encoded version of a captcha code image. Show this image to the user and ask the user to enter the captcha code shown in the image. The captcha code, along with the user's aadhaar number must be sent in the next API.

    Get OTP

    curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/aadhaar/getOTP"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer TOKEN"
  -X POST
  -D '{
    "transID": "TRANS_ID",
    "aadhaarNumber": "USER_AADHAAR_NUMBER",
    "captchaCode": "CAPTCHA_CODE"
    }'

    The API responds with a JSON similar to the following with status code 200: 

    {
  "transID": "TRANS_ID",
  "message": "OTP sent successfully"
}

    Description

    This API sends an OTP on the mobile number linked with the aadhaar number sent in the request of the API. This OTP must be sent in the next API to authenticate the server to access the details associated with the aadhaar number sent in this API. Server then verifies that the aadhaar details match with the details given by the user at sign up.

    HTTP Request

    Request:

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/aadhaar/getOTP

    Headers:

    { "authorization": "Bearer TOKEN" }

    Body:

    { "transID": "TRANS_ID", "aadhaarNumber": "AADHAAR_NUMBER", "captchaCode": "CAPTCHA_CODE" }

    HTTP Response

    The API simply responds with a confirmation message referring that the OTP has been sent successfully to the mobile number linked with the aadhaar number.

    Verify OTP

    curl "${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/aadhaar/verifyOTP"
  -H "Authorization: Bearer TOKEN"
  -X POST
  -D '{
    "transID": "TRANS_ID",
    "otp": "OTP"
    }'

    The API responds with a JSON similar to the following with status code 200: 

    {
  "message": "Aadhaar verification successful"
}

    Description

    This API sends the OTP entered to UIDAI system and receives the aadhaar details and matches them with the details entered by the user at the time of registration. After details are verified, the API responds with a JSON reading that the aadhaar has been verified for the user.

    HTTP Request

    Request:

    POST ${BASE_URL}/AeroMegh/aadhaar/verifyOTP

    Headers:

    { "authorization": "Bearer TOKEN" }

    Body:

    { "transID": "TRANS_ID", "otp": "OTP" }

    HTTP Response

    The API simply responds with a confirmation message referring that the aadhaar details of the user have been successfully verified

    Errors

    AeroMegh APIs uses the following error codes:

    Error Code Meaning
    400 Bad Request -- Your request is missing some required fields/paramters
    403 Forbidden -- Your access token or API keys is invalid. Please check message paramter of the response for details
    404 Not Found -- Your requested resource could not be found
    500 Internal Server Error -- We had a problem with our server. Try again later.

    API IDs

    AeroMegh ML/AI APIs have the following IDs

    API Title IDs
    Social Distancing API 017d50e9-7dd5-4d5f-b1f2-41a1e98eb9e2
    Face Mask Detection API bfd33b5a-2e95-46b8-aae7-0c635c56268e
    Crowd Detection API fc20cad9-bb39-44b3-a5f5-cb87fe39a406

    Env Base URL
    Production https://api.aeromegh.in
    Development http://dev.aeromegh.in:5008
